Important Foreign News

Bank Failures Continue in Various US States 51

In One Year of the Past Year

1,100 Banks Closed

21,000 Companies Bankrupted

Reuters, New York, 3rd Dispatch: Nine more small banks in various parts of the United States closed yesterday.

Reuters, New York, 5th Dispatch: An investigation into the failure of the United Bank has now begun. It is estimated that the bank's debts total about 200 million yuan. Many of the depositors are middle-class people in New York. The Chief Justice stated that the general public has many complaints about the former directors of the bank and questioned why the New York State Bank Supervisor allowed the bank to name itself United, leading simple-minded people to believe it was a government bank. The directors of the bank said that the bank's failure was due to the interference of the Communist Party. Before the bank closed its doors, someone in New York warned depositors by phone to withdraw their deposits quickly.

New York News: The continuous closure of banks in the United States in 1930 was an unprecedented event in the United States. About 1,100 banks closed, with losses amounting to $100 million. At the end of the year, this situation became increasingly dangerous, with several banks closing daily. In Georgia, Indiana, Kansas, Mississippi, and Virginia, seven banks closed on the same day. In Arkansas, nearly 100 banks closed in one month last year, setting the worst record. In addition, the number of bankruptcies of commercial companies also set a new record, reaching 21,712 in eleven months, with losses amounting to $160 million. (World)

European Unemployment Statistics 52

Germany Has the Most, Followed by Britain

National Press, Geneva, 8th Dispatch: The International Labor Office released the number of unemployed people worldwide in December. Germany has the most, exceeding 4 million, followed by Britain with 2.3 million, Italy with 534,000, and Austria with 262,000. Even the city of Danzig has 20,000 people, more than the entire city of Switzerland. Yugoslavia also has 4,700 people. Within Europe, Norway has the fewest, with only 8,000 people. As for the United States, because accurate figures are not easy to obtain, it is approximately between 5 million and 7 million.

Indian Round Table Conference 53

Expected to Conclude Within Ten Days

Reuter's, London, 6th - At today's meeting of the Federal Structure Committee, British Conservative representative Mr. Hoare stated that he could only adopt an unconstrained attitude towards the issue of responsibility for the federal administrative organs. India is now undertaking two major experiments: provincial autonomy and an all-India federation. He would not comment on the central government until the details of the federation plan are more complete than they are today. Liberal representative Lord Reading stated that he agreed with the idea of a responsible government in India, but it must be accompanied by sufficient guarantees to ensure that the government can adequately safeguard the interests of all parties. Indian representative Sapru had proposed a cabinet that is jointly responsible to the legislature, with the departments of national defense and foreign affairs being handled by senior officials appointed by the Governor-General of India. He (Reading) also believed that the Governor-General should have a special power to maintain law and order and to veto any plan passed by the legislature. Conservative Hoare also stated that India is currently unable to defend itself and relies solely on the British army, which can only be controlled by the British government. If there is a Minister of National Defense in the cabinet, how will his responsibility to the British monarch be reconciled with the responsibility of other cabinet members to the legislature? For the sake of ethnic minorities, the Governor-General should retain his special powers. The Indian cabinet will not be a complete cabinet as understood by the British. If the Governor-General is not an effective head of the executive government, how can he exercise the powers reserved to him? Reuters has learned that the reports of the various subcommittees will be submitted by the end of next week, so the Indian Round Table Conference may conclude on January 21st. Most representatives will return to India on the 24th.

Foreign News Roundup 2

Economic Downturn in Britain and America 54

Hitting Hard

New York Tramps Stretching Their Necks for Food

Unemployment Registration Increases in Britain

Lancashire Cotton Industry Strike Trends Towards Seriousness

South Wales Mining Area Negotiations Break Down

Reuter's, New York, 4th - The number of food seekers is increasing daily in the United States. In the streets of New York, there are hundreds of thousands of vagrants without jobs or food. The Communist Party is active in organizing demonstrations demanding improvement of the current situation.

Reuter's, Washington, 6th - Senator Hefflin raised the issue of unemployment and hardship in the agricultural areas of the United States in the Senate today, saying that the situation is critical. If remedies are not provided soon, a revolution will occur. In Arkansas, a large number of farmers have recently attacked cities, shouting for food to save them from starvation. If Congress does not pass the bill to lend 150 million dollars to poor farmers, he will obstruct various government proposals.

Reuter's, London, 6th - The number of registered unemployed people in Britain reached 2.643 million today. This is a new record.

Reuter's, London, 11th - The Lancashire cotton industry strike became more serious yesterday as the Burnley cotton mills began to lay off workers, including 25,000 weavers. Negotiations to resolve the dispute have reached a stalemate. There are currently no meetings, nor any plans for meetings. Reuter's, London, 5th - British cotton mills plan to increase the number of looms managed by each weaver. The weavers are unwilling to accept this. Representatives from both sides met in Manchester on the 2nd, but failed to reach an agreement. This morning, Burnley weavers went on strike to oppose the mills' new system of increasing the number of looms they manage. It is estimated that 3,500 people have been laid off from nine mills that have closed.

Reuter's, London, 6th - Lancashire cotton mills may lay off all textile workers due to the Burnley nine mills strike. If this action is implemented, the number of unemployed workers will reach 500,000. The Burnley mill owners now state that if the strikers do not return to work by next Monday, the mills will dismiss the workers. The executive committee of the British Cotton Textile Industry Federation supports the actions of the Burnley mill owners and has notified all mills in the federation to prepare to close.

Reuter's, London, 9th - The management committee of the Manchester Cotton Spinning and Weaving Association unanimously passed a resolution today stating that if the dispute over increasing the number of looms managed by weavers is not resolved immediately, all mills in the association should be closed on January 17th. This action will leave 200,000 workers unemployed.

Reuter's, London, 9th - The meeting between representatives of mine owners and miners in Cardiff has now broken down because the miners' representatives cannot agree that the independent chairman of the new mediation committee has the right to resolve the issue of wage cuts, holding the view that the issue of wage cuts should be resolved by both parties themselves. Both mine owners and miners have accepted the invitation of the Minister of Trade, Sir Philip Cunliffe-Lister, to meet with mining experts in London on Monday. The South Wales coal region will be shut down for at least another week because even if the two parties agree on terms in London, they must still be approved by representatives from all locations before work can resume.

Reuter's, London, 3rd - 160,000 miners in South Wales oppose the mine owners' method of distributing working hours, and the mine owners are also firmly unwilling to concede. Although the government sent officials on December 31st to mediate and ordered both parties to reopen negotiations, it was ultimately ineffective. Therefore, the miners' union ordered South Wales miners to stop working from January 1st. It is expected that the miners will soon resume work because the union's funds are insufficient and shops are unwilling to extend credit. The mediation committee held a meeting this afternoon, but the miners still firmly opposed the mine owners' proposal, leading to the breakdown of the meeting. The government is now intervening. The Prime Minister, Minister of Labor, and mining experts are scheduled to meet with representatives of the miners in London on the 5th to discuss matters.

Reuter's, London, 5th - Kirk, the secretary of the Miners' Federation, stated that the miners are currently hoping that the government will take action. If the government does not take action, the government's days are numbered. If the South Wales labor dispute is not resolved soon, there may be serious developments nationwide. After the Minister of Labor and mining experts met with the miners' representatives today, the authorities announced that they have summoned the mine owners' representatives to London tomorrow to present everything to the Minister of Labor so that the Ministry can submit a detailed report to the cabinet.

Interest Rate Reduction by American and French Banks 55

Aiming to Curb the Inflow of Funds

No Progress Seen in British-French Expert Meeting

President of the Bank of China in America Expresses::

Opinions on Currency System Issues

Reuter's, London, 3rd - After the New York Federal Reserve Bank reduced interest rates, the French Bank also reduced interest rates to 2%. This is part of a cooperative plan between the United States and France, as the inflow of cash into the United States and France has created a gold shortage elsewhere. Now, reducing interest rates is intended to prevent the inflow of cash. This plan is the result of talks between the heads of the central banks of Britain, the United States, and France. Financial experts from Britain and France are currently meeting in Paris, and further developments are expected. Some have suggested that the United States and France can work to increase outward lending in order to release cash and put Britain in a better position to adjust its industry.

Reuter's, Paris, 10th - The Paris Morning Post states that British and French experts recently met in Paris to discuss the cash issue, but no agreement has been reached. Although France has reduced its bank interest rate to 2% in order to curb the inflow of funds into Paris, the Bank of England, for the sake of its reputation, is unwilling to increase the interest rate to 4%. British financiers want to convene a comprehensive accounting conference to discuss the gold issue, while France prefers direct talks. As the proposal to convene a conference was not established, the British representatives issued a report requesting the Bank for International Settlements to handle the matter. However, another newspaper said that the British-French talks seem to have dispelled dangerous illusions and established a basis for cooperation in order to restore economic activity and better financial understanding. The newspaper also stated that the Young Plan should not be modified, and a systematic method should be established to prevent the overflow of funds, which lies in adjusting interest rates to suit the current situation of the British market.

Reuter's, New York, 8th - Pei Tsu-yi, President of the Bank of China in Shanghai, said in a speech to the American Institute of Mining and Metallurgical Engineers yesterday that the adoption of the gold standard by all countries except China is one of the reasons for the global economic depression. He said that if the currency and financial system are purely backed by gold for a long time, it will inevitably lead to the collapse of the world's financial system because the amount of money owned by each country is not enough to maintain commerce or pay for banknotes. If the world uses more silver as subsidiary currency, the world's silver market can be established on a more solid foundation, and economic depression will not occur so easily. New gold mines have not been discovered. If the annual gold production is not assisted by silver, it will not be able to maintain the expansion of commerce. As for American goods in China, the Chinese may have to pay a higher price due to the low price of silver, but Americans must also greatly reduce prices in order to cater to the Chinese market. The reason why Americans have to make more sacrifices is only to maintain the prestige of gold, their sole standard of value. He is not advocating the use of bimetallism, but feels that the rise in the price of silver can help the recovery of world commerce.

British Fiscal Revenue Shortfall 56

Reuter's, London, 3rd - The Ministry of Finance statistics show that revenue for the nine months ending at the end of December is short by 180 million pounds. In the same period last year, there was a shortfall of 16.9 million pounds. Chancellor of the Exchequer Snowden had predicted a net surplus of over 2 million pounds in the fiscal year ending at the end of March 1931. The current shortfall is so large that the budget outlook is not good.

International Court of Justice Holds Regular Session 57

National News Agency, Geneva, 6th - The International Court of Justice, after re-electing new judges and expanding to fifteen members, is now scheduled to hold its first session in The Hague on the 15th of this month.

Heavy Blow Suffered by Burmese Rebels 58

National News Agency, Bombay, 10th - In Thursday's battle, 39 Burmese rebels were killed and many were injured. The British and Indian military authorities now believe that these people have lost their ability to act after this heavy blow. The British army will continue to be transferred back to its original defense positions.

Ruhr District Coal Mine Labor Dispute 59

Government Orders Arbitration

Labor and Management at a Standstill

National News Agency, Berlin, 10th - The Ruhr coal mine labor dispute came to an end today. The arbitration order organized according to emergency orders has ruled that wages be reduced by 6%. Newspapers speculate that after the coal mine wage cuts are resolved, not only can coal prices fall, but steel prices can also be reduced by 8% soon. The steel industry is scheduled to meet next Wednesday to discuss price reductions.

Reuter's, Berlin, 10th - A recent trend of wage cuts has occurred in the coal mining industry in the Ruhr region of Germany. The mine owners are demanding a wage cut of 8%, while the miners say that the wage cut should not exceed 4% at most. The two sides are at a standstill, causing strikes and Communist Party activities. The President of Germany used his special powers to grant the authorities to arbitrators in order to quickly resolve the labor dispute. The arbitrators have now ruled on a compromise solution, that is, a 6% wage cut, but the mine owners immediately expressed their opposition, and the social miners' union also decided to advise its members to reject the government's arbitration.

Important News

Detailed Account of Mo Teh-hui's Return to China 60

Returned to Harbin on the evening of the 29th at 8:00 PM

Entered the Central Hospital on the 30th

Made a Statement to the Reporters

Harbin Correspondence - Mo Teh-hui, the Chinese Plenipotentiary Representative to the Sino-Russian Conference, returned to Harbin on December 29th at 8:40 PM. Those who returned with him included Secretary Wang Yin-chuan, Zhang Ming-che, attendant Cui Shu-yan, and scribe Sun Su-chen, as well as Mo's wife. The special train they were traveling on, along with the special train that had been dispatched the day before to meet them by various important people in Harbin, consisted of a total of nine cars. The first car was the locomotive, the second and third cars were the baggage car and dining car, the fourth and fifth cars were first-class two-berth sleeping cars for the Eastern Railway Department Chiefs who were dispatched from Harbin to meet them, the sixth, seventh, and eighth cars were official cars for Mo's attendants and Li Shao-geng (Acting President of the Eastern Railway) and others, and the ninth official car was for Mo and his wife. At 8:40 PM on the evening of the 29th, the special train arrived at Harbin Central Station. As the military band played loudly, thousands of Chinese and foreign dignitaries and representatives of legal entities gathered on the platform. In addition to each business firm sending one representative to welcome him, there were also people from Tianjia Distillery outside the port, and the masses from the Binjiang Education Center and Fu'er, who lined up to greet him, holding horizontal banners with slogans such as "Welcome Plenipotentiary Mo's Triumphant Return" and "Welcome Plenipotentiary Mo Who Labored for the Country" and flags with slogans written on them. The Russian dignitaries who arrived included Eastern Railway Council Russian Deputy Chairman Yemushanov, Railway Bureau Russian Director Rudyi, Russian Consul-General in Harbin Melnikov, Council Member Danilevsky, and others, totaling more than ten people. The Chinese who arrived included Zhao Jin-lin, Chief of Staff of the Eastern Railway Protection Army Headquarters, Ding Chao, Garrison Commander of Binjiang, Bao Lian, Director of the Special Zone Political Affairs Department, Zhou Shou-yi, Director of the Education Department, Ying Zhen-fu, Director of the Land Bureau, Jia Wen-qi, Deputy Director of the Special Police Department, Yu Jing-tao, Deputy Director of the Railway Police Department, Wang Li-tang, Council Member of the Navigation Bureau, Wang Shi-ze, Manager, and others, totaling more than a hundred people. Order on the platform was maintained by the Special Police Security Brigade and the Railway Police Guard Squad. All staff members of the Eastern Railway Governor's Office wore usher sashes to assist. After the special train stopped, the crowd gathered under the first special car. Mo stepped down from the car, and the welcoming people waved flags and cheered. Mo nodded in response. After getting out of the car, he entered the VIP room and shook hands with the welcoming people to express his deep feelings. After being seated, tea and fruit were served. Negotiator Zhong Yu rose and delivered a welcoming speech. Mo gave an impromptu speech, which Secretary Zhang Ming-che translated into Russian. He said, "I am honored to be welcomed by everyone at the station today. I am ashamed that I have been dispatched to Russia for eight months, which is not a short time, and I have not been able to fulfill my responsibilities and aspirations after several formal meetings. Fortunately, the past misunderstandings between China and Russia have now been completely understood by each other, and the hope for permanent peace has been completely realized. The conference has now entered a normal track, and continued progress in the future can naturally be smooth. I should have visited you all in person to present everything in detail, but because I have a cold and rheumatism, I plan to go to the hospital temporarily for treatment and plan to go to Beijing in ten days. After I return, I will ask for your advice again." After the speech, they all drank a glass of champagne, took a photo, and dispersed. After leaving the station, Mo did not immediately return home, but first took a car to the Jile Temple in Qinjia Gang to pay respects to the coffin of his deceased wife for a long time. He did not return home until 9:00 PM. On the morning of the 30th, Mo attended the graduation ceremony of the Eastern Railway Rotary Training Institute and gave a lecture. In the afternoon at 3:00 PM, he entered the Central Hospital for treatment and published a notice in the newspaper completely declining all social engagements. He is scheduled to leave on the 5th day of the New Year to first go to Liaoning, then to Dalian Tanggangzi Hot Springs to bathe in the spring to treat his skin disease. He will arrive in the capital around the 15th. For the convenience of the journey, he may go by sea. When Mo's special train arrived in Chita, Russia on the 27th, Harbin had already received a telegram. Li Shao-geng, Acting President of the Eastern Railway, Council Member Shen Rui-lin, Fan Qi-guang, Supervisor Zhang Shu, Kim Rong-gui, Counselor of the Governor's Office, Li Xi-zhen, Director of the Medical Affairs Department, Su Wen-zhong, Director of the Legal Affairs Department, Wang Huan-wen, Director of the Pension Affairs Department, Uze-sheng, Director of the Eastern Railway Library, Zhong Yu, Diplomatic Envoy, and others, along with reporters from various newspapers, totaling more than thirty people, took three cars together at 4:35 PM to meet him in Manchuria. At 9:30 PM on the evening of the 28th, the car Mo was traveling on arrived at the national border from Russia. Many soldiers, police, merchants, and civilians welcomed him at the station. Mo got out of the car and rested in the dining room, chatting with the welcoming people. At that time, there were many Japanese reporters who wanted to see Mo and talk, but Secretary Wang Yin-chuan met with them on his behalf. That evening at 11:21, the special train departed from Manchuria Station. It did not stop at small stations along the way, but people welcomed him at the major stations. Mo originally intended to return to Harbin at around 10:00 AM on the 30th. When he passed Ang'angxi Station on the 30th, he would get off the train to meet with Wan Fu-lin in the provincial capital of Heilongjiang. However, when the train arrived at Boketu Station, Dong Ji-wu, the secretary specially sent by the Heilongjiang Provincial Government, and Wu Zhong-quan, the adjutant, greeted him on behalf of Wan, informing him that Wan had left the province to inspect the army. Since Wan was not in the province, Mo stopped his advance. Therefore, the special train arrived in Harbin half a day earlier than scheduled. When the special train passed Ang'angxi at noon on the 29th, the reporters boarded Mo's special car to talk with him. The questions and answers were as follows: Question: Your Excellency, you have been sent by the Central Government to the Soviet Union for eight months, and you have finally been able to bring the conference into a normal track and proceed smoothly, greatly enhancing the prestige of the Party and the country. There have been various rumors about your return to China this time. What is your mission and when do you plan to go to Russia again? Answer: The Central Government's strategy for the Sino-Soviet Conference at the beginning of the trip was to resolve the Eastern Railway issue. However, due to the needs of the times, the scope of the conference was expanded, and the issues of commerce and diplomatic relations were also discussed. Therefore, I had to return to China to ask the Central Government for specific plans for resuming trade and diplomatic relations so that I could follow them when I went to Russia again to continue the conference. On the one hand, I have been sent to Russia for eight months, and I have held more than 20 formal meetings and informal talks. Although the delegation has reported the situation of the conference to the Central Government at any time, the exchange of documents and telegrams is still not detailed enough. Therefore, taking advantage of the opportunity to return to China to ask for instructions, I plan to report the negotiation process to the Central Government in a more systematic way. In addition, on a personal note, because I have been in Moscow for a long time, I have suffered from rheumatism, and my old skin disease has recently recurred. Because I am often itchy and cannot sleep well at night, I plan to take this opportunity to return to China for treatment. This time, I am asking for a leave of one and a half months, but the round trip takes a lot of time. It is estimated that it will be difficult to return to the Russian capital in the short time of 45 days. At that time, I may have to continue the leave for a few days. But if the Central Government instructs the plan for Russia as soon as possible, I will not delay public affairs. Besides, there is no other mission. Question: The other statements are misunderstandings. Question: Why has the Sino-Russian Conference been delayed for several months? According to various sources, it is said that the conference was suspended due to the dispute between the two sides over the Boli Record in the first few months. Now that the conference is continuing, what is the Soviet Union's attitude towards the Boli Record? Answer: China and the Soviet Union have had very different views on the Boli Record from the beginning. After I went to Russia, the Soviet Union insisted that my country recognize this case, but now it has become a thing of the past. Question: How far have the three issues of the Eastern Railway, commerce, and diplomatic relations progressed so far? Answer: There are two steps in the progress of the three cases of the Eastern Railway, commerce, and diplomatic relations: 1. Formal meetings and negotiations have been announced on the establishment of specialized committees, the allocation of committee members, etc. 2. Informal negotiations have been conducted many times, and both sides have a considerable understanding of various issues, so the opinions are quite close. However, this kind of negotiation is not yet at the stage of publication because it is an informal negotiation. Question: In your observation, is the Soviet Union sincere in this conference? Answer: In principle, this conference is for the mutual benefit of the two countries, so there is no difference in the concepts of the two sides. Since the goals of each other are focused on the interests of both sides, there is naturally no difference in what they hope for. Question: Which item does the Soviet Union advocate to discuss first among the three issues of the Eastern Railway, commerce, and diplomatic relations? Answer: According to conference practice, important issues should be the starting point of discussion. All past disputes between China and the Soviet Union have arisen from the Eastern Railway. Therefore, in terms of nature, the Eastern Railway is the most important of the three issues in this conference. This is the same feeling on both sides and is not a problem. Question: Your Excellency, you have been sent to Russia for eight months. What impressions have you gained? Answer: The Soviet Union is a newly emerging country. Everything is in the creation period. Although the people's lives are not very prosperous, the construction is indeed progressing rapidly, and the spirit of unity and hard work from top to bottom is not to be despised. If the Five-Year Plan is successful in the future, its economy will occupy an important position in the world. Question: When will Your Excellency arrive in Beijing after arriving in Harbin? Or will you have to stay a few more days? Answer: After arriving in Harbin, I plan to see a doctor first and then go to Liaoning and Beijing in ten days. When I arrive in Liaoning, I may have to go to Dalian Tanggangzi Hot Springs for a day or two of recuperation. However, the illness is a personal matter and is not very serious, so I will not delay public affairs because of this. Question: What are Your Excellency's views on the Eastern Railway after returning to Harbin? Answer: The freight rate should be reduced immediately in order to encourage transportation and increase revenue. In addition to layoffs and salary reductions, special attention should be paid to material procurement, engineering construction, and other items to reduce costs. As for the materials used by the Eastern Railway, such as coal and timber, the priority should be given to the railway's own forest farms and coal mines to avoid losses. This is just a temporary remedy. As for the fundamental proposal, there is another detailed plan. On the same day, Mo talked for a long time, but many of them were diplomatic secrets and could not be disclosed. The reporter also asked whether the Eastern Railway team of the Sino-Soviet Conference would continue as usual after his return to China. He said that it would be temporarily suspended and would be held at the same time as the other two teams after he asked for instructions and returned to Russia. (December 30)

Postponement of the Implementation of Abolishing the Likin Tax in the Northeast 61

Commander Zhang sent a telegram ordering a three-month extension

Changchun Correspondence - The National Government recently issued an order to all provinces to implement the abolition of the likin tax and similar likin-like transportation surcharges on January 1st of the 20th year. After receiving this order, the Northeast provinces had to consider how to make up for the sudden loss of a large amount of revenue due to the fiscal relations of each province being self-sufficient, and the implementation procedures also had to be planned in the long term. After Commander Zhang discussed with the Central Government to request an extension of three months for preparation, he telegraphed the Northeast provincial governments from Tianjin on the Ma day of last month, saying, "Previously, the deadline for the abolition of the likin tax was urgent. I telegraphed the Ministry of Finance on Qiao day to request an extension of three months. I have now received a reply telegram from Minister Song of the Ministry stating that I have been informed of the Qiao Lei case regarding the three-month extension of the abolition of the likin tax in the northern provinces. I have asked the National Government to meet and inform you. I am sending a special telegram to inform you." Therefore, none of the Northeast provinces implemented the abolition of the likin tax on New Year's Day. They are now waiting for Zhang's return to the East to convene a giant meeting to determine the plan. (January 5)

Northeast China Will Realize Water-Land Intermodal Transport 62

Goods shipped from Tianjin can directly reach Harbin

Resisting the Manipulation of the South Manchuria Railway and the Chinese Eastern Railway

Harbin Correspondence - After the four railways in the Northeast implemented intermodal transport, goods from Tianjin and Shanghai can now be directly transported to Liaoning and Jilin. However, goods from northern Manchuria have always been gathered and distributed in Harbin. Although the four railways have been transported to Jidong and Heilongjiang by intermodal transport, they still have to go through the South Manchuria Railway operated by Japan and the Chinese Eastern Railway jointly operated by China and Russia. The freight rates of both railways are in gold, and the rates are surprisingly high, resulting in prices in northern Manchuria being more than twice as high as those in southern Manchuria, especially for salt. Last winter, Huang Zhen-gang, a shipping merchant on the Songhua River, proposed the establishment of a shipping consortium to expand shipping routes and compete with Russian merchants by advancing into the Heilongjiang and Ussuri rivers in a unified manner to avoid competition. This matter has now been initiated and is expected to succeed soon. However, ships that go downstream have deeper drafts. It is planned to open up new routes for ships with shallower drafts. Before the New Year, the Shipping Association sent personnel to the Qiqihar-Taonan Railway to investigate. The railway sent engineers and technicians to cooperate in surveying at the confluence of the Nenjiang and Songhua rivers. It was measured that the riverbank at this location is flat and wide, with natural stone cliffs and a water depth of 11 units at normal times, which can accommodate shallow-draft steamships. If a branch line of the Qiqihar-Taonan Railway is extended from the Dalin line, it will be about 40 li long and can directly reach the river mouth. Then domestic products can be transported through the intermodal transport of the four railways without having to be transferred by the South Manchuria Railway and the Chinese Eastern Railway to reach the Nenjiang River mouth and then transported by ship to Harbin. If the goods are shipped from Tianjin, the route is Beining, Datong, Siping-Taonan, Taonan-Angangxi, and the upper reaches of the Songhua River. It is estimated that the freight can be saved by 20%, and the salt alone can save 2 million yuan per year. The freight of the South Manchuria Railway and the Chinese Eastern Railway and the upper reaches of the Songhua River can increase the freight by 2 million yuan. Other goods have not yet been calculated. The time can be shortened by five days. Therefore, after the intermodal transport of water and land is realized, it is not only the financial resources of the Songhua River Customs that will increase, but also the national economy and the people's livelihood will also benefit greatly. This matter has been approved by the Northeast Transportation Committee. In the future, the Taonan-Angangxi Railway authorities and the Songhua River Shipping Association will jointly discuss it. Recently, the Songhua River Shipping Association has launched Gao Wen-xuan, Sheng Yin-xiang, Zheng Zi-zhan, Ma Yu-liang, Wang Ming-shan, and Liu Xi-san as audit freight committee members to discuss the freight rules from the Nenjiang River mouth to Harbin and submit them to the Taonan-Angangxi Railway for approval in order to implement them. (5th)

This matter has been approved by the Northeast Transportation Committee, and in the future, the Tao'an Road authorities and the Songhua River Shipping Association will jointly discuss it. Recently, the Songhua River Shipping Association has launched Gao Wenxuan, Sheng Yinxiang, Zheng Zizhan, Ma Yuliang, Wang Mingshan, and Liu Xisan as audit freight committee members to discuss the freight rules from the Nenjiang River mouth to Harbin and submit them to Tao'an Road for approval in order to implement them. The Legislative Yuan's 125th Meeting 63

The Revised Organization Law of the Ministry of Industries Passed

The Legislative Yuan held its 125th meeting at 8:00 AM on the 10th. The committee members in attendance were Liu Guanxun, Luo Ding, Shi Shangkuan, Lu Fuzhonglin, Zhao Shibei, Liu Kejun, Wu Shangying, Zhu Luhe, Zhang Mojun, Li Shuhua, Zhu Hezhong, Xi Chaojun, Liu Jingxin, Peng Yangguang, Lu Zhiyi, Lin Bin, Chen Changheng, Shi Weihuan, Fang Juehui, Wu Tiecheng, Wei Huai, Liu Shirun, Sun Jingya, Cai, Feng Zhaoyi, Dai Xiujun, Huang Youchang, Niu Yongjian, Ma Chaojun, Zhou Wei, Jiao Yitang, Wei Tingsheng, Lou Tongsun, Chen Ying, Zhang Fengjiu, Deng Zhaoyin, Wang Baozhen, Zhu Jingsong, and Zhuang Songfu, totaling 39 members. The chairman of the meeting was President Hu Hanmin.

(A) Matters for Report

(I) Reading of the minutes of the 124th meeting.

(II) The National Government's instruction No. 2334, regarding the promulgation of the Fourth Book of the Civil Code, Family Law, and the Fifth Book of the Civil Code, Inheritance Law.

(III) The National Government's instruction No. 2335, regarding the promulgation of Chapters 1 to 5, Section 3, of the Civil Procedure Law.

(IV) The National Government's instruction No. 2386, regarding the promulgation of the Amnesty Law for Political Prisoners, including the attached schedule, and the order to the Executive Yuan and the Judicial Yuan to take note.

(V) The National Government's instruction No. 2388, regarding the promulgation of the revised regulations for the management committee of Sun Yat-sen's Mausoleum.

(VI) The National Government's instruction No. 2367, regarding the promulgation of the Farmers' Association Law.

(VII) The National Government's instruction No. 2401, regarding the Regulations for the 20th Year of the Republic Tobacco Tax Bonds and the Repayment Schedule.

(VIII) The National Government's approval of the sixth matter discussed at the 123rd meeting of the Legislative Yuan and referral to the Civil Service Department for investigation, as notified to the Executive Yuan.

(B) Matters for Discussion

(I) Review of the Civil Service Appointment Law and its Implementation Law. It was resolved to submit it to the Legislative Committee for review and drafting.

(II) Revision of the organization and establishment law of the Military Council. It was resolved to submit it to the Legislative and Military Committees for review.

(III) The Executive Yuan urged the drafting of various cooperative regulations. It was resolved to have the original drafting committee member, Lou Tongsun, expedite the drafting.

(IV) The Legislative Committee reported on the interpretation of whether the lowest-ranking appointed officials, whose performance after screening and review is rated as Grade C and have no lower grade to be demoted to, should be converted to probation or dismissed. It was resolved to pass the review report and dismiss them.

(V) The Legislative Committee reported on the review of the Postal Administration Regulations and the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau Regulations, and requested the designation of committee members to draft the Postal Savings Law and the Domestic Remittance Law. It was resolved to postpone the decision.

(VI) The Legislative Committee, in conjunction with the Economic Committee, reported on the review of the draft Organization Law of the Ministry of Industries. It was resolved to revise and pass it.

Tan Daoyuan Defeats Zhu and Mao at Zhongcun 64

All Departments in Jiangxi Ordered Not to Rest on New Year's Day

Zhang's Division Engages in Fierce Battle with Communist Bandits in Donggu

Tan's Division Kills Several Thousand Communist Bandits in Zhongcun

Nanchang Communication: Lu Diping, Director of the Nanchang Headquarters and Commander-in-Chief of the Ninth Route Army, issued a general attack order on Zhu and Mao's bandit gangs on the 30th of the year's end. He also ordered all units suppressing bandits in Jiangxi not to rest on New Year's Eve or New Year's Day in order to eliminate the communist bandits as soon as possible. Therefore, while the whole country rested and celebrated the New Year, the bandit suppression troops continued to fight the communist bandits in the border areas of Xingguo, Ningdu, Jishui, Ji'an, and Yongfeng. The fighting was extremely fierce. According to recent news from the front, the left wing of the bandit suppression troops, Zhu Shaoliang's Mao Bingwen Division, advanced towards Ningdu after recovering Guangchang on December 24th of the past year. The right wing, Jiang Guangnai and Cai Tingkai's divisions, advanced towards Xingguo after capturing Taihe and Wan'an, adopting a pincer movement encirclement strategy. At the same time, the central route, the Ninth Route Army's Zhang Huizan, Gong Bingfan, and Tan Daoyuan's divisions, launched attacks from Yongfeng, Ji'an, and Le'an through Donggu to the south, targeting Zhu and Mao's main base, Gulonggang (located at the border of Xingguo County, Ningdu and Yudu). The communist bandits, fearing encirclement from all sides, made a desperate gamble. Zhu De's fake Fourth Army, Huang Gonglue's fake Eighth Army, Mao Zedong's fake Twelfth Army, Chen Yi's fake Twenty-second Army, and small gangs led by Hu Zhusheng, Li Shaojiu, Duan Yuequan, and others, totaling about 70,000 to 80,000 men with guns, launched an attack on the 18th Division of the government army on New Year's Eve and New Year's Day. Zhang Huizan, the division commander, Dai Yue, the deputy division commander, and Wang Jiejun, the 53rd brigade commander, personally led their troops to the front line to supervise the battle. They fought a bloody battle with the bandits at the border of Yongfeng, Xingguo, and Jishui, charging back and forth in melee combat, which was unprecedentedly fierce. However, on the 2nd and 3rd of this month, a heavy fog suddenly descended, making it impossible to distinguish directions in the high mountains and ridges. Many government soldiers were unfamiliar with the terrain, while the communist bandits were very familiar with the terrain, especially those from Yudu and Xingguo, and the peasants who had been transformed into bandits acted as guides. Therefore, the bandit army launched a large-scale offensive, and the 52nd and 53rd brigades of the 18th Division were surrounded by the communist bandits, struggling to break through. The Gong and Tan divisions, which were supposed to provide reinforcements, were also unable to reach them on time due to the heavy fog and unfamiliarity with the terrain. After running out of ammunition, the Wang and Dai brigades fought with bayonets, suffering heavy casualties and losses. There were also reports that Donggu had been retaken by the bandits and that Division Commander Zhang and Brigade Commanders Wang and Dai were missing. However, a key figure in the Ninth Route Army headquarters stated that the 18th Division had been ambushed by the communist bandits but had only suffered minor losses, and that the outside reports were not true. In this battle, Zhang's division also killed countless communist bandit fake division commanders, regimental commanders, battalion and company commanders, and bandit soldiers. Later, Tan Daoyuan's 50th Division rushed from Le'an and encountered the communist bandits in Zhongcun, killing several thousand bandits and seizing more than 2,000 guns, defeating the communist bandits. The communist bandits retreated to Ningdu. The 18th Division also returned to the Jishui area on the 3rd for reorganization. In addition to ordering the Gong and Tan divisions to continue their attacks and advance, coordinating with the 6th and 19th routes, and setting a deadline to break through Gulonggang, Lu Diping, fearing that the communist bandits would attempt to riot during the New Year, ordered the garrison headquarters to be on strict alert in order to consolidate the security of the rear of Nanchang. All game venues were closed on the 4th, and the independent 14th brigade, under Liu Yi, was stationed to defend the city walls. Therefore, the provincial capital was very peaceful. (6th)

Military Affairs in Xuzhou During the New Year 65

Wang and Han's Divisions Reorganized into Class B Divisions

Recent Situation of Defense and Transportation

Xuzhou Communication: All circles in Xuzhou celebrated the New Year with great enthusiasm after the military had been pacified. The troops stationed in Xuzhou also implemented a scaled-down reorganization during the New Year period. The details are as follows:

New Year's Celebration: On New Year's Eve of the 19th year, Xuzhou experienced heavy snowfall. On New Year's Day, the weather cleared up. At 9:00 AM, all circles held a celebration meeting at the public club, attended by approximately 10,000 people. Liu Tianzhan, Chairman of the County Reorganization Committee, presided over the meeting. Representatives from various agencies and organizations, as well as representatives from the 7th and 52nd divisions, delivered speeches. In the afternoon, entertainment activities were held, including Beijing opera performances by the Zhengfeng Society and new dramas by the Mingshi School. National flags were hung throughout the city, and slogans were posted everywhere. Businesses were closed for five days, from New Year's Day to the 5th. The common people performed dramas such as flower boats, stilt walkers, and lion dances, parading through the streets, which was very lively. It was also decided that all celebrations and entertainment activities during the lunar New Year would be prohibited in order to promote the national calendar.

Military Reorganization: The 7th and 52nd divisions stationed in Xuzhou were reorganized into Class B divisions, each division consisting of two brigades and six regiments. The reorganization began on New Year's Day. The 7th Division originally had three brigades, the 19th, 20th, and 21st, each brigade consisting of two regiments. It is now reorganized into two brigades, each brigade consisting of three regiments. Chen Xueshun, the commander of the 20th Brigade, was relieved of his command and will be assigned to another position. The two regiments under his command were incorporated into the 19th and 21st brigades, respectively. The 52nd Division originally had two brigades, each brigade consisting of three regiments. Zhang Zhongdiao's 154th Brigade has already completed its reorganization in Xuzhou. Sun Changjun's 155th Brigade has been temporarily unable to reorganize due to its deployment to Jiangxi to suppress the communist bandits. Both divisions are being reorganized according to the Class B division organization promulgated by the central government. The total number of officers and soldiers in each company is 109. The wartime stretcher-bearer platoon and transportation platoon have been eliminated. The special service battalion has been changed to a supply battalion, and the communications squad has been merged into the engineer battalion. The units directly under the division, in addition to the division headquarters and various offices, include two brigades, a artillery battalion, a supply battalion, an engineer battalion, and a cavalry company. However, the 52nd Division still retains a supplementary regiment pending reorganization.

Defense Situation: The defense of Xuzhou City was originally the responsibility of Zhang Zhongdiao's 154th Brigade of the 52nd Division. As of today (8th), it has been changed to the responsibility of Zeng Wanzhong's 19th Brigade of the 7th Division. Wang Jun, the commander of the 7th Division, went to Beijing to visit Chiang before the New Year and has not yet returned. Han Deqin, the commander of the 52nd Division, went to Beijing on the 2nd to visit Gu Zhutong and returned to Xuzhou on the 5th. It was heard that Wang had telegraphed the Third Army Headquarters in Xuzhou, informing them of the order to abolish the Jinpu Garrison Command and reorganize it into the Jinpu Police Headquarters to handle garrison affairs. There are rumors that the entire 52nd Division will be transferred to Jiangxi to suppress the communist bandits. However, after the reorganization of the various units, the headquarters has sent personnel to Xuzhou to verify the numbers. It seems that they will not be transferred until after the verification.

Transportation Situation: There have been no changes in the time schedules for the Liaopu Railway, the Blue Steel Car, and the express trains on the Jinpu Railway. The Longhai Railway has recently stipulated the train schedules for each section. Between Xuzhou and Luoyang, there will be three special express trains per week, leaving Xuzhou every Monday, Wednesday, and Friday at 8:00 AM and arriving in Luoyang every Tuesday, Thursday, and Saturday at 8:20 PM. Between Xuzhou and Zhengzhou, there will be daily passenger trains, leaving Xuzhou every morning at 10:00 AM and arriving in Zhengzhou every evening at 6:03 PM. Between Xuzhou and Haizhou, there will be daily passenger trains, leaving Xuzhou every morning at 8:40 AM and arriving in Haizhou every evening at 6:04 PM. All trains on the Longhai Railway connect with the trains on the Jinpu Railway, making transportation in all directions extremely convenient. (8th)

What's Happening in Jinan During the New Year 66

Han Fuju Returns Vehicles to Various Railways

Jinan Municipal Government Orders Abolishment

Jinan Communication: The New Year of the 20th year of the Republic has passed swiftly amidst enthusiastic celebrations from all sectors. There are two major issues in Jinan during this New Year that are worthy of recording. One is Han Fuju's return of vehicles to various railways, and the other is the Jinan Municipal Government's order to abolish itself. Regarding the return of vehicles, the Ministry of Railways sent Qian Tangchao (Longhai Railway), Tang Dehua (Jinpu Railway), and Wu Shangzhi (Jiaoji Railway) as supervisors to oversee the return of vehicles by various military units. In addition, various railways sent personnel, including Zhu Quan (Secretary, Jinpu Railway), Wei Xinping (Section Chief, Jiaoji Railway), Chen Qitang (Section Chief, Pinghan Railway), Jin Jingshan (Longhai Railway), and Lv Yunxun (Section Chief, Longhai Railway). Han Fuju appointed Zhang Lianjia, the Director of the Public Relations Office, to be responsible for handling the return of vehicles. After Zhang consulted with the Ministry of Railways, it was decided that one locomotive and thirty passenger and freight cars would be temporarily retained for the Third Route Army's military transport, which had not yet been completed. The remaining locomotives and passenger and freight cars would be returned to the various railways. By the 4th, all procedures for the return of vehicles had been prepared. On that day at noon, Han Fuju and Zhang Lianjia hosted a banquet at the Shi Qinyan Hotel for the personnel from the Ministry of Railways and various railways who were handling the return of vehicles, as well as Lv Zhenting (Section Chief, Jinpu Railway), Shun Qiguang (Station Chief, Jinan Station), Tang Weicheng, Liu Dide (Section Chief, Jiaoji Railway), Du Baotian, and Kong Guangxun (Station Chief, Jinan Station), among others. The banquet was very convivial. After the banquet, the vehicle return was carried out. The Jinpu and Jiaoji Railways issued receipts to the two railways, which were then distributed to other railways. A total of eight locomotives and one hundred fifty-nine passenger and freight cars were returned. The detailed numbers are as follows:

(A) Returned to the Jinpu Railway: (I) Six locomotives, including Pinghan Railway No. 611, No. 203, No. 623, Zhongxing Company No. 56, Jinpu Railway No. 30, and Jiaoji Railway No. 70. (II) One hundred thirty-two passenger and freight cars. Those returned at Jinan Station totaled two hundred and five, including twenty from the Pinghan Railway, twenty-eight from the Jiaoji Railway, four from the Bianluo Railway, thirteen from the Jinpu Railway, fourteen from the Beining Railway, ten from the Pingsui Railway, three from the Longhai Railway, four from the Daoqing Railway, and two from the Zhongxing Company. Those returned at Xinzhuang totaled twenty-one, including seven from the Pinghan Railway, two from the Pingsui Railway, five from the Jinpu Railway, two from the Huningyong Railway, two from the Jiaoji Railway, one from the Beining Railway, one from the Bianluo Railway, and one from the Longhai Railway. Those returned at Dezhou Station totaled three, including one from the Pingsui Railway, one from the Jinpu Railway, and one from the Jiaoji Railway. Those returned at Jining Station totaled one from the Pinghan Railway. Those returned at Tengxian Station totaled one from the Jiaoji Railway. Those returned at Pukou Station totaled one from the Jiaoji Railway.

(B) Returned to the Jiaoji Railway: (I) Two locomotives, including Pinghan Railway No. 201 and Jiaoji Railway No. 509. (II) Twenty-seven passenger and freight cars. Those returned at Jinan totaled twenty-four, including nine from the Pinghan Railway, one from the Pingsui Railway, two from the Jinpu Railway, one from the Zhongxing Company, seven from the Beining Railway, three from the Jiaoji Railway, and one from the Daoqing Railway. Those returned at Zuoshan Station totaled two, and those returned at Fangzi Station totaled one, all of which were Jiaoji Railway cars.

(C) Temporarily Retained: (I) One locomotive, Pinghan Railway No. 509. (II) Thirty passenger and freight cars, including nine from the Pinghan Railway, seven from the Longhai Railway, six from the Pingfeng Railway, four from the Pingsui Railway, two from the Jinpu Railway, one from the Bianluo Railway, and one from the Daoqing Railway.

Regarding the Jinan Municipal Government's abolishment, the reason was financial difficulty after the abolition of likin. However, the accidental burning of explosives during the burning of drugs by the government on December 29th of last year, which resulted in the death and injury of a large number of civil servants, was also a reason for the abolition. After the incident occurred, the public and various party and government agencies were deeply dissatisfied with the municipal government and the public security bureau. The punishment of those responsible was the focus of attention from all sides. The provincial government also believed that the matter was of great importance. Although Mayor Chen Weixin and Public Security Bureau Chief Wang Zunwu were not intentional, they could not shirk their responsibility for negligence. Therefore, on the 6th of this month, a clear order was issued to remove Mayor Chen Weixin from his post (after consultation with the authorities on the 8th, he was appointed as a provincial government advisor as a face-saving measure). Wang Zunwu, the Chief of the Public Security Bureau, was transferred to the provincial government as an advisor. At the same time, because the municipal government had not made any achievements in the past year and was in extreme financial difficulty, it was decided to abolish the municipal government. The various bureaus under the municipal government, including the Public Security Bureau, the Finance Bureau, the Education Bureau, the Public Works Bureau, and the Social Affairs Bureau, were all placed directly under the provincial government in order to facilitate administration. Wang Kai, the Director of the River Affairs Bureau, was appointed to replace Wang Zunwu as the Chief of the Public Security Bureau, and Zhang Lianjia was appointed as the Director of the River Affairs Bureau. Wang and Zhang took office at 2:00 PM on the 6th. After receiving the order, the municipal government worked to hand over its affairs, with the section chiefs consulting with Xing Lanjie, the receiver appointed by the provincial government, on all matters. The notice of the abolishment of the municipal government is recorded below: "In accordance with the Provincial Government's Instruction No. 15, due to financial constraints after the abolition of likin, the Jinan Municipal Government is hereby abolished. All administrative affairs of the said government are to be merged into this government for concurrent management in order to save expenses. The various bureaus originally under the municipal government, which have specific responsibilities, shall continue to exist and be directly under the jurisdiction of this government. You may proceed directly to the relevant agencies to handle all administrative matters of this government relating to public security, health, social affairs, education, public works, finance, and land. This is hereby announced. January 1, 20th year of the Republic. Mayor Chen Weixin."

The Enthusiasm of Various Provinces in Celebrating New Year's Day 67

Nanchang Nanchang Communication: In order to expand the promotion of the national calendar and enthusiastically celebrate the founding of the Republic of China, the Nanchang All-Circles Celebration Preparatory Committee for the 20th Anniversary of the Founding of the Republic of China was established. Representatives from the General Headquarters Second Propaganda Brigade, the Ninth Route Army Headquarters, the Provincial Party Department, the Provincial Government, the Municipal Party Department, the Municipal Government, and various industrial, commercial, and academic organizations served as preparatory committee members to carry out all activities. The committee originally intended to hold a citizens' assembly on New Year's Day, but after receiving a telegram from Lu Diping from the front lines, it was decided that during the period of bandit suppression, it was appropriate to share weal and woe with the refugees in the bandit areas and not to overspend. Therefore, it was changed to a representatives' assembly. On the morning of New Year's Day at 10:00 AM, a celebration meeting was held at the Provincial Party Department, attended by over a thousand representatives from all walks of life. At 7:00 PM, a lantern parade was held, which was extraordinarily lively. On the 2nd and 3rd, Beijing opera and new dramas were performed at the public stadium for two days. On the evening of the 4th, the mayor freely performed dragon dances and there were many flower lanterns. A large number of people watched the fireworks display at Donghu. As for the merchants and people, many closed their accounts at the end of the year and rested for three days from the 31st. The shops pasted couplets and hung lanterns in front of their doors to celebrate. (5th)

Fuzhou Fuzhou Communication: This year, various party and government agencies actively promoted the national calendar and promoted it. Therefore, the celebration of New Year's Day this year was very enthusiastic. At 9:00 AM on the morning of the same day, the party, government, military, police, business, academic, and women's circles of the provincial capital held a New Year's Day celebration meeting at Nanqiao. At 2:05 PM, they departed and paraded to Nantai, distributing the national calendar and various propaganda materials. The Xiamen aircraft also circled in the air at 2:00 PM, distributing slogans. (6th)

The First Day of the Jiangsu Provincial Pacification Conference 68

Resolved to Divide into Groups to Review Proposals

The Jiangsu Provincial Pacification Conference was held yesterday (the 10th). The opening ceremony was held at 10:00 AM on the morning of the same day. Chairman Zhang Zhijiang performed the rituals. Zhang then reported the purpose of the conference, followed by speeches by Ma Yinbing and Ye Chucang. Finally, music was played and photos were taken, and the opening ceremony ended. After the opening ceremony, Zhang Zhijiang specially prepared seven tables of Chinese food to entertain the attending members and the press. Ye Chucang occupied the first seat in the central table, Ma Yinbing the second seat, Li Houji (guest) the third seat, Li Mingyang the fourth seat, Lu Changgeng the fifth seat, Liang Guanying the sixth seat, and Zhang Zhijiang the seventh seat. When the banquet was half over, Zhang Zhijiang stood up and said, "I am very happy to be gathered here with you today. I recently heard Chairman Ye say that he saw slogans promoting the welfare of the people in the streets and was truly afraid to accept them, but he dared not refuse to take responsibility for the people. In the cold weather, the gentlemen who have come to the meeting have not spared their precious time to gather together and express their great opinions. Isn't this for the benefit of the people? I, your humble brother, am in the position of host and have prepared a small meal to offer my respects." Ye then delivered a speech, and the host and guests were extremely congenial. After the banquet, they rested briefly and then began the meeting at approximately 3:00 PM. Forty-five people attended the meeting, and eleven people were present as observers. Ye Chucang presided over the meeting and performed the rituals. After reading the rules of the Pacification Conference, Chen Zhuoru, the Chief of Staff of the Governor's Office, reported on the pacification work and the recent important bandit situation in Jiangsu. Then, Lan Bohua (representative of Tongshan County), Huang Jialin (representative of Taixing), Shen Shaochang (representative of Haimen), and Wu Changkui (representative of Suqian) reported on the bandit situation in their respective counties. It was originally planned to continue discussing the proposals, but because the time for rest had arrived and there were many proposals, it was decided to divide into groups to review the proposals. The proposals were divided into five groups for review: clearing the countryside, self-defense, searching and suppressing, rehabilitation, and other. The members of each review group were appointed and will be discussed further after they are categorized in the days to come (11th).

Hangzhou Quick Dispatch 69

The Zhejiang Provincial Agricultural and Mining Department was yesterday handed over by Director Qian Tianhe to the Construction Department for management. The affiliated institutions of the department include more than ten places such as agricultural, forestry, sericulture, fishery, animal husbandry, and cotton fields. Director Shi of the Construction Department changed the fourth cashier's section of the department to the fifth section, and the various agricultural and mining affairs are handled by the fourth section, which has now started working.

Since Zhejiang Province implemented the abolition of likin on January 1, the number of goods transported from the five stations of the Hangzhou city gate, Nanxing, Hangzhou Genshan, and Gongchen to Shanghai has increased several times. Every time the company's freight cars arrive in Hangzhou, the goods unloaded at the station pile up like mountains. As a general rule, the likin tax paid directly to the Finance Department by each company every ten days has now been stopped.

The draft of the Zhejiang Business Tax Collection Act contains 25 articles. The amount of tax payable by each industry listed in the act is enough to enrich the provincial treasury, but it is still doubtful whether each industry can afford to bear it. It has been learned that the silk industry guild estimates that the business tax will be 30 per mille, reaching about 400,000 yuan per year, which is less than 100,000 yuan different from the original voluntary donation. Adding in the consolidated tax, the silk industry will find it difficult to maintain the status quo. Four representatives have now been appointed to petition the Finance Department, stating the situation and requesting that the draft be revised to benefit the business.

The Hangzhou Municipal Chamber of Commerce previously drafted six rules to ban competitive sales by businesses in various industries and submitted them to the Municipal Government for approval. It was decided that they would be implemented from the first day of this month. Currently, more than ten shops, including foreign goods and department stores, are not complying with the rules and are arbitrarily engaging in competitive sales. Yesterday, Pan Xieqing was sent to give them a warning first. If they still do not comply, the Municipal Government will be requested to strictly prohibit them (11th).

Local Communications

Jinshan 70

Bandits are Rampant Again in Qinshan Kongjia Que. The area of Qinshan Kongjia Que has always been a place where bandits emerge. Since the anti-smuggling team patrol boats were stationed in Kongjia Que last summer, they have been somewhat restrained. Unexpectedly, at the end of the year, the bandit forces have become rampant again. Robbery and kidnapping occur frequently. On the night of December 30, more than a dozen bandits suddenly came to the house of Sun Shuigeng, a farmer in Qianshan East. They broke into the house with torches and searched the house at will. Because there were no valuables, they tied up Shuigeng and his mother, beating them until their bodies were covered in injuries. On the night of the 31st, the families of Gao Caisheng and Maosheng, about half a mile north of Kongjia Que, were also robbed. They even kidnapped the five-month-old child of Caisheng and Fushan and asked for 3,000 yuan in foreign currency within three days to be sent to Tangjia Bridge. Also, on the evening of January 5th, bandits suddenly appeared in the houses of Zhu Yiyi and Ruizhi in Kongjia Quexi Shanzu. Dozens of people with guns held weapons in their hands. After arriving at the door, the bandits fired their guns as a warning. The wife of Yizhai, Mrs. Yu, who was nearly ancient, was shot in the vital part of her body and died. Ruizhi's son, Qiyun, was taken out by the bandits for more than a mile before he was released after begging. This is also a great fortune in misfortune. It is estimated that the stolen clothing and accessories were worth about four or five hundred gold. When the anti-smuggling team stationed in Kongjia Que heard the alarm and went to chase, the bandits had already gone far away.

Songjiang 71

Public Prosecution Filed in the Tragic Death Case of Hu Zhang. At the beginning of the establishment of the County Court, the case of the Hu surname in Da Wuqiao plotting to kill his wife caused a sensation in the whole city. The Procuratorate immediately arrested Hu Yinglong and his aunt Hu Nie for investigation and supervised the officials to open the coffin for examination. After several investigations by the Procuratorate, the public prosecution was filed. It is heard that the indictment states that Hu Yinglong had premeditated the crime. In the quiet of the night, in the inner chamber, there was no one else. Therefore, Hu Yinglong could not shirk the responsibility of suspicion. Moreover, according to the confession, he had slightly twisted her with minor suspicion before the incident, and finger and claw marks were found on the neck of the body. The Criminal Court of the Court held a hearing on the 9th to investigate everything. It is heard that Hu Yinglong and others have hired lawyer Zhang Baopei to defend them. The Court has scheduled another date for public debate.

The Security Regiment Conducts a General Cleaning. Cao Pang, the commander of the Second Regiment of the Jiangsu Provincial Security Team, led his team to station in Songjiang. In addition to training in January, he also noted that there were many pits and accumulated garbage in Songcheng. He advocated on the 3rd, when various groups gathered for a New Year's dinner, that the troops should clean up the segments in sections. The proposal was supported by the public. The First District Office provided a large number of brooms and baskets and ordered the departure this morning (11th), personally leading the cleaning. Although the cold wind was strong and the ground was covered with ice and snow, they were spirited and courageous. At that time, the whole city was illuminated. It is heard that the police will also hold regular meetings to promote this initiative.

Ancient and Modern Calligraphy and Painting Exhibition. The Art Department of the First Public Education Center in Puzhao Temple in the city has now obtained the consent of various collectors in Songjiang and writers from the Songfeng Calligraphy and Painting Society to open an exhibition of ancient and modern calligraphy and paintings in the department from the 13th of this month for one week. It is heard that the ancient painting section will be exchanged every two days, all of which are rare and valuable masterpieces. At that time, there will be a grand occasion.

Suzhou 72

Preparatory Committee for the Sun Yat-sen Memorial Hall in Wuxian: The Preparatory Committee for the Sun Yat-sen Memorial Hall in Wuxian held its fourth general meeting on the afternoon of the 10th. The fundraising committee, divided into 25 groups, reported the names of the elected heads and deputy heads of each group. It was then decided that the collected donations would be managed by the Guohua and Xinfu banks. The method for soliciting designs was also approved before the meeting adjourned.

Proposal to Establish a Wireless Radio Station: The Su-Ge long-distance telephone system was originally established to facilitate bandit suppression. However, in the event of major bandit attacks, the telephone lines were often damaged by bandits. Recently, specialist Chen Zongtai submitted a proposal to the Construction Bureau, requesting the establishment of a wireless radio station in Suzhou, with four branch stations set up at key locations such as Jiaozhi and Dongshan. The estimated initial cost is over 29,000 yuan, with a monthly operating cost of 600 yuan for the main station and 300 yuan for each branch station. A detailed plan was submitted to Director Wei of the Bureau, who praised the plan. Yesterday (the 11th), he approved it, awaiting consideration and implementation.

Preparing for the Journalists' United Association: The Suzhou Journalists' Association is preparing to reorganize the Wuxian Journalists' United Association. Meetings will be held every Sunday to carry out preparations.

Wuxi 73

Request to Abolish the Special Silk Cocoon Tax: The Silk Factory Guild of this county stated that after the silk cocoon tax was ordered to be abolished, the Ministry of Finance intended to introduce a special silk cocoon tax. Factory silk is a major part of foreign trade. China is based on agriculture, and silk cocoons are originally a by-product of farmers. Since factory silk has been sold to Europe and the United States, silk cocoons have become a major item for increasing national economic strength. In recent years, the European and American silk markets have been controlled by Japanese merchants, and the business of Chinese merchants has plummeted. The only way to reverse the failure of the silk industry is to eliminate all taxes and reduce the cost of factory silk. This will allow Chinese silk to compete with Japanese silk and have a chance of winning. If a special silk cocoon tax is reintroduced, it will directly increase the burden on silk merchants, indirectly reduce foreign trade, and shrink the national economic strength. Therefore, the guild sent a letter to the County Chamber of Commerce yesterday, requesting it to forward the letter to the Ministry of Finance and quickly abolish the proposal to levy a special silk cocoon tax, in order to maintain international trade and give silk merchants a glimmer of hope. After receiving the letter, the County Chamber of Commerce stated that factory silk is a major part of foreign trade in China, which seems to be different from other silk. In recent years, the cost of factory silk in foreign trade has been too high to compete with Japanese silk, which is indeed the main reason. If taxes can be eliminated to reduce costs, it may be a way to encourage improvement. Therefore, the chamber immediately forwarded a telegram to the Ministry of Finance, requesting it to consider and approve the matter.

County Government Burns a Large Quantity of Opium and Gambling Paraphernalia: Pan Geng-sheng, the county magistrate of this county, recently discovered that a large number of opium and gambling paraphernalia had been seized and stored on record. From the time of his predecessor to his own tenure, up to December 24th, a total of 1,087 cases of opium pills and gambling paraphernalia had been seized. Yesterday afternoon at 5:00 pm, all the opium pills and gambling paraphernalia stored on record were piled up in front of the county government's auditorium and burned in public. At the same time, the magistrates of Wuxian and Kunshan counties dispatched section members to Wuxi to supervise the proceedings, as instructed by the Civil Affairs Department and the High Court, to show solemnity. An Appeal to Reduce Interest on Pawned Items: The Pawnbrokers' Union of this county stated that Article 16 of the Jiangsu Provincial Government's Regulations on the Pawnbroking Industry stipulates that if a pawned item is redeemed more than five days after the expiration date, the interest should be reduced by half a month; if it is redeemed more than fifteen days, the interest should be reduced by one month. Yesterday, they sent a telegram to the pawnbrokers' unions of various counties, urging them to jointly appeal to the government to postpone the implementation of Article 16 of the Provincial Regulations on the Pawnbroking Industry.

Jiangyin 76

Two Cases Prosecuted: On August 15th of last year, the Jiangyin Fortress District and the County Police Force seized a case in the Yangtze River involving Chen Bing-quan, platoon leader of the former 20th Battalion of the 5th Water Police District, and others smuggling opium. Chuan Chun-sheng, Sun Ze-hai, Sun Bai-shuang, Li Gui-ru, Wang Da-mao, Wang Xiao-mao, Cai Xiao-erzi, Cai Zi-cheng, Xin Xiang-jin, Xu Ying-he, and Xu Jia-cai, Xu Xiao-erzi jointly transported military firearms without permission and cannot prove that it was for legitimate reasons, and are suspected of violating Article 42 of the Criminal Code and Article 2, Paragraph 1 of the Military Firearms Control Ordinance. Wu Jing-xian Kidnapped in Lishui, Now Safe: Wu Jing-xian, the former administrative committee member of the 2nd District of Danan Township, was kidnapped by bandits while collecting winter rent in Lishui last year and was extorted for 45,000 yuan. The Six County Party Representatives Gathered in Nantong to Discuss Provincial Party Affairs: Zhang Yuan-yang, a provincial committee member, and instructor Cheng Ru, gathered representatives from the party committees of six counties, Nantong, Rugao, Haimen, Qidong, Jingjiang, and Taixing, in Nantong on the afternoon of the 9th to decide that the party committees at all levels in each county must complete reorganization within February. The Business Situation in Tongyi Last Year: The Nantong business is centered on cotton yarn and cloth. Nantong suffered a poor cotton harvest in 1930. The yarn market was extremely sluggish, and the total transaction volume of native cloth was 10 million yuan, only 60% of that in 1929. As a result, various industries were not prosperous. In the Tangzha industry, the Dasheng Yarn Factory accounted for the most profits, with more than 700,000 yuan. The Dasheng Sub-Factory in Jiangjiaqiao earned 320,000 yuan. Almost all yarn industries in the city were at a loss. The financial sector was not at a great disadvantage due to prudent lending. The foreign goods industry suffered heavy losses, and Xinchangzhuang and others have gone bankrupt.

Two Fishermen Kidnapped in Baojiaba: In Baojiaba, Juegang District, Rugao, on the night of the 4th, many pirates suddenly came and kidnapped two fishermen, Bao Guangli and Bao Jinsheng. Gaoyou 80

Farmers and Grain Merchants Robbed by Bandits: More than 20 bandits armed with guns broke into the home of farmer Bian Yong-yu in Huayuan Township of the county on the night of the 4th, looting everything and shooting and wounding farmer Zhu and farmer Shen Liu. Grain merchant Liang Jincheng went to Huaiyi County to purchase grain the other day. When the ship reached the Er Maqiao of Gao Shaohu, a boat suddenly jumped out with three male bandits and one female bandit, each holding a box cannon and ordered them to stop. Hangzhou 81

Opening Up of Sanmen Bay Has Begun: The opening up of Sanmen Bay in Zhejiang Province is related to the livelihood of the people and the wealth and strength of the country. Previously, merchant Xu Ting-zu requested to pledge his assets to the government to borrow 500,000 yuan in public bonds to contract for the opening up of the bay. The central government and the Zhejiang Provincial Investigation Department have jointly surveyed and designed the matter. However, the Ministry of Finance felt that the financial aspect was impossible to think about because military affairs had just been settled and there were many things to be handled. Xu also understood this situation, so he has raised funds from overseas Chinese and started the first phase of the project. In addition to the seawall and dam projects that have already started construction, he is also planning the reclamation area to relocate farmers for spring ploughing.

The Various Bureaus of the Construction Department are Streamlined into Sections: Shi Ying, Director of the Construction Department of Zhejiang Province, has implemented a tightening policy for the affiliated institutions of the department. It has now been decided that the entire streamlining plan will be implemented. In addition to the decision to abolish the Electrical Bureau, the highway, railway, water conservancy, telephone, agriculture and forestry, and navigation bureaus will all be converted into sections. The internal organization must not exceed four divisions. As for the operating expenses of each section, they must be re-planned and submitted for approval. A proposal has been drafted to be passed at the next provincial government meeting and implemented.

The Loan of Two Million Yuan Has Been Settled: After several rounds of consultations, the Zhejiang Finance Department decided to borrow two million yuan from the banking sector yesterday, using a combination of one million yuan from the remaining Zhejiang Provincial Construction Bonds, ninety thousand yuan from the central treasury bills, and forty thousand yuan from slaughter taxes. Apart from the twenty thousand yuan temporarily borrowed last December, which has been paid off, the remaining 1.8 million yuan will be paid in four installments, starting from the 15th of this month as the first installment payment date. Each installment will be 450,000 yuan, and all payments will be made by February 15th. The contract will also be signed on the 15th.
