Educational News

Important News

Ministry of Education Orders Dissolution of 82

Association for Continuing Supplementary Geng Funds for Students Studying in Japan

In order to resist Japan's cultural aggression against China, the Ministry of Education, together with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, had been working to abolish the Agreement on Japanese Cultural Undertakings in China, which was signed between the former Beijing government and Japan. In July of last year, the Ministry of Education ordered the Supervisory Office for Students Studying in Japan to stop recruiting students with supplementary Geng funds to show its determination to abolish the agreement. Recently, Gao Qian and other self-funded students studying in Japan organized the Association for Continuing Supplementary Geng Funds for Students Studying in Japan, requesting the Ministry of Education to restore the supplementary Geng fund quotas and distributed leaflets that were widely published in newspapers. It is reported that the Ministry of Education has specifically ordered the Supervisory Office for Students Studying in Japan to inform the students that the government is seeking to abolish the Sino-Japanese Cultural Agreement and that the supplementary Geng funds have not been restored. The original order is extracted as follows:

It has recently been found that Gao Qian and other students studying in Japan have submitted a report to the Ministry of Education in the name of the Association for Continuing Supplementary Geng Funds for Students Studying in Japan, requesting permission to restore the supplementary Geng fund quotas for students studying in Japan. At the same time, they have also printed and distributed the "Letter to All Circles of the Association for Continuing Supplementary Geng Funds for Students Studying in Japan" and published it widely in newspapers. They have completely disregarded the Ministry of Education's intention to stop the supplementary Geng fund quotas in order to abolish the Sino-Japanese Cultural Agreement. It should be known that before this negotiation is resolved, it is extremely difficult to restore the supplementary Geng fund quotas. Moreover, when these students went abroad, they were required to raise sufficient funds for their entire study abroad expenses in accordance with the regulations. How can they rely solely on this? In view of the above, you are hereby ordered to immediately comply with the order and report the dissolution of the association for filing.

Ministry of Education Explanation 83

The Formal Style of Communication between Education Bureaus and Education Associations

Should Use "Order"

The Education Bureau of Huaining County, Anhui Province, requested clarification on the formal style of communication between the county education bureau and the county education association, as it was incomplete. The regulations of the Education Association and the Ministry of Education's Order No. 1087 of the 18th year of the Republic of China specified that the Education Association should use "report" when communicating with the Education Bureau, but there were no clear regulations on the Education Bureau's communication with the Education Association. Therefore, the Anhui Education Department was requested to interpret the matter. The Anhui Education Department, because the matter involved the interpretation of laws and regulations, forwarded it to the Ministry of Education for instructions. It is reported that the Ministry has interpreted the instructions as follows: "All provincial, municipal, and county educational administrative organs should use 'order' when communicating with subordinate education associations."

Ministry of Education 84

Approves Registration of Private Schools and School Boards

The Ministry of Education recently issued a notice to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities regarding the private schools and school boards that were approved for registration in November and December. The list of school names and school boards is as follows: (Jiangsu) Jiangyin Zhengcun Junior High School, Wujin Zhengheng Junior High School (Shanghai) Da Xia University Affiliated High School (Zhejiang) Hangzhou Huixing Junior High School, Muxing Junior High School (Anhui) Bengbu Jianghuai Junior High School (Shandong) Jinan Aimei Junior High School, Yuying Junior High School (Hunan) Changsha Xiuye Agricultural School (Hankou) Lianghu Junior High School School Board (Rehe) Chaoyang Zhinan Normal School School Board

Ministry of Education 85

Explains the Competent Authority for Student Self-Government Associations

The Education Department of Jiangsu Province requested the Ministry of Education to interpret whether student self-government associations should be under the respective jurisdiction of county and municipal governments, in accordance with the Implementation Rules of the Organizational Outline of Student Self-Government Associations promulgated by the central government. It is reported that the original text of the Ministry of Education's interpretation is as follows: "Article 6 of the Implementation Rules of the Organizational Outline of Student Self-Government Associations states: 'When the student self-government association has completed its organization, it must submit its constitution, resume of officers, and list of members to the local senior party department for approval, and then report to the school and the competent authority for record.' According to this article, the student self-government associations of schools at all levels in the provinces and cities should be under the respective jurisdiction of the municipal and county governments, and their constitutions do not need to be submitted to the Provincial Education Department for approval."

The Reorganization of the Zhejiang Education Department is Complete 86

Zhang Nanxian Encourages the Staff of the Zhejiang Education Department

Since the new director of the Zhejiang Education Department took office, the reorganization has been completed. There have been few changes to the original staff, and they have all remained in their original positions to maintain familiarity. However, there are three secretaries, one section chief, six section members, four clerks, and one secretary who need to be appointed due to his succession. The newly appointed secretary is Qian Jia-zhi (transferred from supervisor), Li Bang-shou, fourth section chief Zhang Yiyang, section members Qi Xiaoyong, Ruan Yi-bing, Zhang Guanghan, Shou Chong-shu, Zhang Zhe-hui, Xie Shou-ruo, and clerk Chen Yi-ru. Director Zhang specially reduced the size of the auditorium slightly and expanded the left and right sides to make it usable. The dismantling and manufacturing are currently underway.

Zhang Nanxian, chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, recently went to the Education Department to inspect and discuss the progress of education in the province with Director Zhang. He also summoned all the secretaries, section chiefs, and supervisors to give instructions, saying that the work of the agency depends on the collective wisdom and strength, and hoped that they would work together to eliminate all obstacles and make the education of Zhejiang Province develop day by day. The educational funds should be raised by the Finance Department so that there would be no delays in the future, so that they could be expanded.

The Director of Agriculture and Mines Bureau Visited the County Farm

Fa Fan Qie Er broke through the defense with incredible speed. Bote Lan instinctively raised both hands, believing the ball had gone out of bounds. However, it miraculously entered the net. Thus, the Xu team finished the first half with a 2-1 lead over the Gu Shi Tai team, turning the match into a draw.

After switching sides, the game's momentum shifted slightly. The Gu Shi Tai team launched several counterattacks, displaying considerable activity. Zhou Xianyan bravely dove to block it, but unfortunately, it went in, resulting in a 2-2 tie, adding another layer of tension. Free Talk New Rhapsody for New Year's Day - Heaven, Void, Me, Life

People get up late on the solar New Year, the people's spirit is high, and the calendar is low. What can be seen in the six streets and five markets? National flags are hung at the doors of every household. The rice paper is dyed bright red, printed with couplets for the New Year. The sound of gongs and drums is like thunder, and the fast cars rush through the streets. The guest houses in West Lake are full, like a long holiday during Qingming. The tea houses and restaurants are crowded with people, and those who come are often unexpected. Gamblers have always feared the police, but today they are acting as gamblers. Sharing happiness with the people should be the case, and serving the country is also in this regard. Don't you see the storytellers sitting high in the hall, their oily hair sweating and their voices hoarse? They painstakingly want to win the laughter of thousands of people, but what harm is there in relaxing the ban for a day? The old people in the countryside tell each other that the world is truly strange today. They pick up burdens and go into the city in the morning, but no one cares about the big and small scales. They don't see delicate maids calling along the street, only mischievous children playing. The market keepers are with hot dogs, and the beggars in the flower market are dressed as fake lions. They can't get enough to eat without money in the middle of the day, and the green vegetables are about to rot. Life is short, enjoy it in time, quickly call your wife and children, don't raise two sows, don't feed five hens. People have already celebrated the New Year, why are you and I still suffering from hunger? Failure to collect rent is a mistake, and letting go of the New Year is rare. I think the sages have ancient teachings, and what the people like, we should like too. Just look at the faces of the spring breeze guests, already smugly happy. It turns out that governing the country and pacifying the world can be done by letting them do it without letting them know.

Record of the Strange Stones of Jiaoshan Mountain

Jiaoshan Mountain stands tall in Jingkou, and its beautiful scenery has always been famous. The Zhou Dynasty Ding, the Han Dynasty Drum, and Yang Wenxiang's jade belt have been repeatedly seen and spoken of by predecessors. However, the strange and beautiful stones have been hidden among the ordinary, and have not been praised by tourists. This is often the case in the world. I am writing this to introduce them to future tourists.

There are eight stones, four in each place. Three are secretly placed in Jiaoshan, and the rest are placed in the Wenchang Pavilion. The ones secretly placed in Jiaoshan are said by the monks to have been brought from Han Dynasty by a certain official of the Qing Dynasty. The stones are similar in size, about two inches long and wide. One is like a portrait of a beauty in ancient costume, with delicate and charming facial features and slightly blurred features. The hair seems to be covered in a light gauze. One is like a boat with masts, sails, and hull complete, slowly moving in the middle of the stream, fitting the poetic meaning of "a wild ferry with no one, the boat crossing by itself." One is like a plum blossom, with soft branches, slender branches, and abundant flowers, very similar to the potted plants in Suzhou, showing a charming attitude towards people. One is like an image of the God of Longevity, with a towering forehead, long beard, and wide robes, leaning on a cane. The ones in the Wenchang Pavilion are larger than the previous ones, and the texture is also delicate. The images are particularly lifelike. One pattern is like a clump of bamboo, with the Bodhisattva Guanyin reclining under the green bamboo shade. The beauty of the image and the naturalness of the posture are extremely admirable. The rest are a plum blossom, a Zhong Kui, and a landscape. The plum blossom has ancient branches, gnarled branches, and buds about to bloom. Zhong Kui has a red face, bristling beard, bent arms, and wide eyes, extremely vivid. The landscape has a natural layout, sparse and distant, like the brushstrokes of Qing Xiang's Bada. The monks said that Chiang Kai-shek had also visited and observed the stones, pointing to a black spot on the top of the stone and saying to his entourage, "If this point were changed from black to ochre or white, then this stone would be priceless." It is said that ochre resembles the sun and white resembles the moon. The monks also said that these four stones are half artificial, unlike the ones secretly placed in Jiaoshan, which are completely natural. When Sun Chuanfang resisted the Northern Expeditionary Army in Jingkou, he used artillery to bombard Elephant Mountain, collapsing a corner of the mountain. The monks then brought back the collapsed stones with strange patterns and processed them to obtain these shapes. (Que Chou)

Mr. Zhu Shenghu from Fengxian

Zhu Shenghu, whose style name is Jichen, recently changed it to Jicheng, for reasons unknown. He is the second son of the poet Li Lianyou, who is known for his elegant and refined style. Zhu Shenghu is quiet and withdrawn, rarely smiling, and seems out of place in the world. He keeps his room clean, burns incense, and sits quietly, like an ancient recluse. However, when he meets kindred spirits, he becomes warm and courteous, with proper manners. When he is happy, he laughs loudly, startling everyone around him. He is skilled in painting and calligraphy, and is especially proficient in seal carving. His running script follows the style of Yan Zhenqing and Huang Tingjian, with a strong and upright style. His brushstrokes are like a swordsman carrying a sword, or a strange pine tree with beautiful rocks, displaying a proud and resolute spirit. His clerical script originates from Zhang Qian and Heng Fang, incorporating the brushstrokes of the Wan Sou, which are profound, simple, and full of changes. Like an old vine in an ancient garden, its roots are intertwined. The traces of the Xiang crossing the river are like meditation. His painting style is similar to Yun Jiang's, elegant and free from vulgarity. He doesn't make many ugly paintings, and few people understand him. His seal carving follows the style of Wan Bai and Bei An, with moist white characters and strong red characters. His successful works directly pursue the Qin style. He loves solitude and silence, and his walls are covered with famous calligraphy and paintings. He focuses his mind and meditates, learning from the ancients. He is different from modern writers who chase fame and fortune, and bow down to the wealthy. Therefore, his name is not well-known, and few people understand him. The old plaque of his residence, Rong Yu Tang, is said by those who know it to be better than Su Kan's, and not just empty praise. Great mountains breed pearls, and hidden jades contain glory. How can a gem remain hidden forever? Will those who know Mr. Zhu not forget him?

Aerial Torpedo Boat Fu Cun

The American Cole Dubonnet planned to create an aerial torpedo boat after the European War, and it is now ready and undergoing testing. This boat can travel on land, sea, and air. The boat's design is similar to ordinary airplanes, except that instead of wings, it has a huge dish-shaped rotating wheel installed on top of the entire boat, like an umbrella. Its engine is a Carsley engine, installed in the center of the entire boat. The entire boat is made up of three boats combined into one. The middle boat is the largest, and the engine is installed in it. The two boats on the left and right are smaller and are used for passengers. The rear of the boat also has a tail, which is about the same length as an airplane. The end of the tail is equipped with a rudder, which is also a smaller rotating wheel, but one is installed vertically and the other horizontally. When flying in the air and descending, the dish-shaped rotating wheel stops rotating, and its function is like a parachute, very stable and comfortable. The bottom of the boat is boat-shaped, so it can float on water. When it wants to land on land, the two small boats on the left and right that carry passengers have movable wheels, one on each side, which can be retracted and lowered at will. According to the inventor, Dubonnet, the gasoline required for this boat to ascend is less than that of other airplanes, it is more stable to ride, and the cost is also very low. Currently, two prototype boats have been manufactured, and the test results are very satisfactory. The edge of the dish-shaped wheel of one of the boats is made of a trumpet-shaped air duct, which uses air to push out from the inside, thereby rotating the entire wheel.

A Review of the Year in Film Miao Xiu

The year 1930 has passed quickly. Here, I want to make a simple review of the domestic films of the year. I think this is a good lesson, or it can make people inside and outside the film industry work together to promote domestic films.

Although there are quite a few domestic film companies in Shanghai in name, compared to the number of productions, only the Mingxing Film Company has produced more. It is rare to see other companies produce more than ten films. However, at least 300 foreign films have been brought to Shanghai for their initial release. Domestic films have only produced a maximum of 100 films. On the one hand, it can be seen that the leakage of films is not small. On the other hand, it can be seen that domestic films are still in their urgent struggle period.

However, if we look at the box office records of several famous films, we feel that domestic films also have the opportunity to revive. According to a survey, since the arrival of sound films in Shanghai, foreign theaters in Shanghai have rarely been able to make money. On the one hand, it has been affected by the price of gold. On the other hand, it is due to the language barrier. It is better to watch domestic films such as Hong Lian Si and other films that have always maintained the faith of the masses.

Parisian Tales (1) Six Once Upon a Time in Paris

An Old Film in a Small Cinema

Now, sound films can be considered to be at their peak in Paris. The large cinemas near the Opéra, the most lively place in Paris, play only sound films every day. These sound films mostly have many musical and dance interludes. Of course, there are good ones, but I think most of them are very mediocre and too trendy. Sometimes, because the director doesn't know how to handle it well, there is loud shouting in places where silence is needed, which is really disappointing.

I don't completely dislike sound films, but sometimes I think silent films are more interesting. In silence, we can carefully appreciate the actors' facial expressions and all their actions. If our palace needs musical stimulation, I think a real band is better than the dumb sound passed through a microphone. For example, when the screen shows a romantic encounter under the moon and flowers, if a real violinist slowly plays a soft tune, wouldn't that be more interesting and poetic than the noise of these sound films?

But if you still want to savor outdated silent films in Paris now, you must not go to the large cinemas on those grand Boulevards to ask. You can try your luck in the small cinemas in the Latin Quarter for four or five francs, or you might still be able to find them.

There are many small cinemas in the Latin Quarter, mostly for students to pass the time. Naturally, there are also small businessmen and workers inside. The tickets for these small cinemas are very cheap. You can get a decent seat for about five francs. From Monday to Friday, there are not many people. Only on Saturdays and Sundays is it really crowded. If you don't buy a ticket in advance, you sometimes have to queue at the door for an hour to get in.

These small cinemas also play sound films a lot, but they still retain a part of the effort of silent films. If you are lucky, you can sometimes see very good films. If you want to get unexpected satisfaction at a very small price, then the small cinemas in the Latin Quarter can really be said to be a very suitable place to pass the time.

Now, I will talk about an unremarkable silent film that I recently saw in a small cinema in the Latin Quarter that made me satisfied. Welcome, it can be seen that domestic films have a new way out in this era of sound films.

The most memorable thing in this year is the creation of Chinese sound films. "Wild Grasses and Leisurely Flowers" is only a partly dubbed sound film, but it can be regarded as a prelude. And what we should pay the most attention to is that the fully sound film "Songstress Red Peony" released by Mingxing Company can also be performed in the near future. It is expected that domestic films after this can be more full of new interest and vitality.

In short, in the past year, it has been very difficult for Chinese films to maintain their inherent position in society. Fortunately, Heaven has given a good opportunity. In the near future, it will definitely be able to reawaken the enthusiastic belief of our people in domestic films because of the release of the domestic sound film "Songstress Red Peony". Then, I hereby wish "the 20th year of the Republic of China will be the era of the development of domestic films."

Recorded by Xiao Yuan, narrated by Chen Xianrong

Yesterday, a friend sent a letter from Luo Yue, mentioning that there was an old man there who could understand the language of apes. Therefore, I have recorded this for readers' entertainment.

Luo Yue is a remote and isolated region, thousands of miles away from the Central Plains. In the past, it was a place where the virtues of the sage kings could not reach, and a den of poisonous snakes and fierce beasts. Fish, monkeys, apes, and the like often appeared together, which troubled the scholars. In Xiao Sha (a small village in Luo Yue), there was an old man who was old in age but energetic. He disliked socializing and was dull and incompetent. However, he could understand the language of apes and communicate with them. Jiao Jiao Ai Ai was his specialty. One day, a group of apes came out to trample on the crops, which was unbearable. The scholars asked the old man for help. The old man immediately went to the group of apes, blew his reed tongue, and strongly advised them not to worry about the crops. The apes obeyed and retreated. Therefore, the crops of the scholars were safe, so everyone praised his merits.

The author notes that what my friend said may not be fictional. In ancient times, the officials of the Yi Li tribe were in charge of communicating with birds, and the officials of the He Li tribe were in charge of communicating with beasts. Jie Ge Lu could understand the mooing of cows, and Gongye Chang could recognize the language of birds. There have been such things for a long time. Only the section where the old man persuaded the apes not to disturb the crops seems absurd and unfounded. I hope that there are often mysterious and incomprehensible things in the world. I will just record it.

Warmth in My Heart (347) Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 16: Earnestly Asking for Words, Emerald Sleeves Visit the Teacher; Generously Discussing Military Affairs, a Heroine's Banquet in the Brothel

Now, the hairstyle of that Ms. Ren Peizhen is not some Chaoqian style or Xiangda style, nor is it the current Fengliang style or Huanxin style. That hairstyle is somewhat like the one worn by Japanese women, with a circle of hair covering the surroundings. The Japanese call it "Kasa." When Ren Peizhen walked into the room, the eyes of everyone in the room, unintentionally and naturally, focused on her alone. Not only did the people in Luyi's room seem to see someone with strange clothes and a strange language, but even the singers who were called in were a little surprised to see the chest-thumping, belly-protruding female hero come in, and they whispered to each other. When Zuo Shichen saw her come in, today he was the host and should fulfill his duties as the host, so he stood up and greeted her and asked her to take a seat. Although the people present knew that she was the famous female revolutionary Ren Peizhen, they had never met her before. This was because Mr. Sun Qilei first introduced the host of today, Zuo Shichen, and then introduced all the people present. Moreover, that Ren Peizhen had a strange temper. Although she was a woman, she did not like people calling her "Ms." She said that since men and women were equal, why should women be specially labeled with the word "woman"? A scholar is a scholar, why distinguish between men and women? If a woman is called "Ms.," it is obvious that there is some discrimination against women. She called the people who were with her in the revolution at that time "comrades." Therefore, many people called her "Comrade Ren Peizhen." As for casual acquaintances, they would call her "Mr. Ren Peizhen." She said that the two words "Mr." are the best, and there is no distinction between men and women in terms of their meaning. Sun Qilei had already notified the people present in advance to call her "Mr. Ren," and even the people in the room had already been told to call her "Mr. Ren." Otherwise, based on her age and appearance, she should of course be called "Madam." In fact, she had never formally married, and according to the rules, she could only be called "Miss." But Ren Peizhen was not like a "Miss" at all, and the title of "Miss" inevitably had some corruption. It was common to call her "Mr.," especially in the Tangzi, they would never call a woman "Mr." as a special thing, because their leather makers also called women "Mr.," and distinguished between "Big Mr.," "Small Mr.," and "Sharp Mr.," and so on, so it could be considered popular. At that time, everyone called her "Mr. Ren," asked her to take a seat, and gave her the highest seat. She humbly declined and said that this seat was not good to sit on, everyone else had come later. Besides, Mr. Ren was a female hero of our Republic of China, a great revolutionary. We have admired her for a long time, and it is a great honor to be able to look up to her here today. That Ms. Ren did not decline too much. She was always generous, so she politely took the head seat.

Local News Situation of Customs Revenue and Expenditure in the Republic of China in 1919

Approved and Released by Finance Minister Song

According to the National News Agency, the report on the situation of customs revenue and expenditure in the Republic of China in 1919, submitted by General Customs Commissioner Meller, has been approved and released by Finance Minister Song, as follows:

The total amount of customs duties (import duties, export duties, re-import duties - transit duties in and out of the interior, and ship taxes) in the Republic of China in 1919 was 18,057,000 taels of customs silver. There are three methods of calculating the above tax revenue:

(1) 1,663,000 taels of customs silver (equivalent to 17,616,000 yuan in customs gold units) is the tax revenue collected according to the gold unit tariff. The actual amount of gold units received is 17,616,000 yuan.

(2) 10,568,000 taels of customs silver (equivalent to 120,091,000 yuan in customs gold units) is the tax revenue collected according to the gold unit tariff. The calculation method is based on the price of gold and silver at any time. The actual amount of customs silver received is 10,568,000 taels.

(3) 5,826,000 taels of customs silver is the tax revenue collected according to the customs silver tariff. The actual amount of customs silver received is 5,826,000 taels.

The total amount of the above three items is 18,057,000 taels of customs silver.

The following table details the actual amount of tax revenue from various important customs offices in 1919 and the increase or decrease compared with the tax revenue in 1918 (calculated in whole numbers):

Customs Name Tax Revenue in 1919 Increase (compared with 1918) Decrease

Harbin Customs 1,900,000 taels of customs silver 788,800 taels

Antung 4,134,000 taels 343,000 taels

Dairen 12,234,000 taels 110,300 taels

Newchwang 3,400,007 taels 1,321,100 taels

Tientsin 13,226,000 taels 3,000,900 taels

Kiaochow 9,181,000 taels 1,510,000 taels

Hankow 7,497,000 taels 767,000 taels

Shanghai 86,743,000 taels 17,200,000 taels

Amoy 3,457,000 taels 1,280,000 taels

Swatow 4,918,000 taels 1,990,000 taels

Canton 9,713,000 taels 3,500,800 taels

The total amount of regular customs duties managed by the General Customs Commissioner in the Republic of China in 1919 was 6,547,000 taels of customs silver (calculated in whole numbers).

All principal and interest on foreign debts, indemnities, and rehabilitation loans secured by customs duties have been paid in full, totaling 12,773,952.95 yuan in customs gold units (equivalent to 13,241,637.27 taels of standard silver), and 78,232,712.04 taels of standard silver, for a total of 91,474,349.31 taels of standard silver. Compared with the amount paid in the Republic of China in 1918 (65,336,113.41 taels of standard silver), this year's actual expenditure was 26,138,235.90 taels of standard silver more.

Principal and interest on domestic debts and treasury bills secured by customs duties and returned Boxer indemnity funds have also been paid in full.

Wang Zhengting Returned to Beijing Yesterday

Going North to Tianjin Today and Planning to Go to Peking

Participating in the Ceremony to Receive the Belgian Concession in Tientsin

Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting took the night train to Beijing at 11 o'clock last night. According to an interview with a reporter from this newspaper at the train station, he plans to accompany Xu Mo and Diao Minqian to Tianjin tomorrow (i.e., today) to participate in the ceremony to receive the Belgian Concession in Tianjin. He also plans to visit Peking on the way. He expects to return to Beijing in about a week. The Sino-Japanese Ning case has been basically negotiated, and a formal signing can be done after one or two more meetings. The replies to the Six-Nation Legal Rights Conference have been delivered to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, except for Brazil, which has not arrived due to the long distance. The meeting is now scheduled to continue in February.

Taxpayers' Association Pays Attention to Public Security in the Concessions

Letter to the Public Works Bureau and the Chairman of the Board of Directors

The Taxpayers' Association sent a letter to the Public Works Bureau yesterday, requesting strict investigation of theft cases, stating, "We are writing to you because Huaitong Company stated in a letter that they had read the newspaper and learned that your association had sent a letter to the Public Works Bureau complaining about their lack of effort in preventing bandits. We are very grateful for this. Unfortunately, our company was also robbed at 7 a.m. on the 22nd of this month. A week has passed, and we have been inquiring with the police station every day, but there has been no news. This shows the ineffectiveness of the bureau's work. Our company is not a large merchant, but a small business. The loss from this accident will make everyone feel insecure in the future if there is no day when the truth comes out. All taxpayers in the concession should have their safety protected. The amount of the robbery suffered by our company is about 6,000 yuan, which is not a small amount. We will now present the situation of the robbers at that time. On the 21st of the month, which was a Sunday, six robbers suddenly came at 7 p.m. They spoke in various dialects. Five of them held guns and went upstairs, while one held a gun downstairs to monitor the tea servants and others. They arbitrarily ransacked the boxes and baskets, robbing everything. They robbed 2,300 yuan in Bank of China banknotes, 500 yuan in silver dollars, and milk beads, pearl rings, gold and silver jewelry, etc., worth about 3,000 or 4,000 yuan at the negotiated old price, for a total of more than 6,000 yuan. We reported to the old police station and asked them to investigate. They sent detectives to inspect and inquire at our company, but a week has passed, and there have been no results. Our colleagues are strangers in a foreign land, and they have no way to seek help. We earnestly ask for your assistance and ask the police station to solve the case as soon as possible to reassure the people."

The letter also stated that the association had sent a letter inquiring whether the bureau had the ability to maintain public order due to the frequent kidnapping cases, and that the director of the bureau had made a statement to the Greater American Evening News on December 27, saying that it was because the victims did not report to the police station. The association now stated that the director's statement was completely fabricated, otherwise why would the case have been reported to the police but no progress had been made in the investigation so far. It is appropriate to send a letter to your bureau to check and order the case to be strictly investigated and solved quickly to reassure the people.

Correcting Fei Xindun's Remarks The association also sent a letter to the chairman of the Public Works Bureau, stating, "We are writing to you because kidnapping cases are frequent and even result in deaths and injuries. On December 26 of last year, we sent a letter to your bureau asking whether you have the ability to maintain public order, etc., but we have not received a reply. Unexpectedly, we saw that the director of your bureau, Fei Xindun, made a statement to the Greater American Evening News on December 27, and his remarks were very irresponsible. His statement that one policeman cannot be assigned to each household is even more nonsensical. The director holds an important position and should think of ways to ensure the safety of all taxpayers in the city and fulfill his responsibilities. Taxpayers are unwilling to hire someone who only makes irresponsible remarks and serves as a decoration to the municipal government with a huge annual salary. It is appropriate to send a letter to you, hoping that you will check and correct him quickly."

Edward's Case Against the Public Works Department to be Tried Within a Month 91

The Shanghai Times reports that Public Works Department General Manager Edward has filed a complaint with the Consular Court against his unwarranted dismissal by the Public Works Department. The Public Works Department's response was submitted to the court by its representative lawyer yesterday afternoon (the 10th), but its contents will not be disclosed for the time being. It is rumored that this case involves significant issues, so the Consular Court has deviated from its usual practice by adding two additional consuls to jointly preside over the trial. It is expected to commence within a month at the latest. Edward is seeking a monthly salary of 1,500 taels until the contract expires in September 1932, as well as first-class passage back to England for his entire family, a retirement pension, an additional 5,000 pounds in damages for his reputation, and reimbursement of court fees for five trials. His complaint stated that he previously received a letter from the Public Works Department stating that they were not interested in renewing his contract due to his poor performance.

Regulations for Indoor Wiring for Electrical Users in This City 92

Notice from the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau 93

The Municipal Public Utilities Bureau issued a notice on January 9th, stating: "For the purpose of announcing that, following an order from the Municipal Government, the Construction Committee was consulted and found that the electrical industry in our country has been developing rapidly in recent years. The installation of indoor electrical wiring and all safety equipment should be subject to regulations to ensure compliance. After reviewing the domestic electrical industry, and consulting the practices of various countries, this bureau has formulated forty-five regulations for the installation of indoor electrical wiring, along with seven appendices. It has been stipulated that the regulations will take effect on January 1, 1931, and have been promulgated by bureau order and submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval on record. In addition to issuing separate orders to the construction departments of various provinces and consulting them separately, corresponding regulations are hereby enclosed for your government's review and requested promulgation, and for directing all subordinates to comply accordingly."

It further attached regulations to the government. The bureau issued a separate order instructing electrical companies to comply and give public notice.

An investigation reveals that these regulations pertain to the current methods of installing indoor electrical wiring. These regulations are similar in nature to the "Regulations for Indoor Wiring for Electrical Users in This City" previously promulgated. However, the former only covers the installation of electrical lighting wires, while the latter includes both electrical lighting wires and power lines. Now that the Construction Committee, as the central government's competent authority, has promulgated the above-mentioned regulations, the regulations of the same nature promulgated by this city in the name of the local government should be abolished. However, regarding the methods for installing indoor power lines, the provisions of the "Regulations for Indoor Wiring for Electrical Users in This City" pertaining to power lines will continue to apply until the central government promulgates rules. This matter has already been submitted to the Municipal Government for record. This notice is hereby given for public knowledge.

Supplementary Notes on the Opening of the Zhongshe on New Year's Day 94

The Zhongshe, after half a year of preparation, officially opened on New Year's Day. At 9:00 AM on that day, members and guests gathered in the assembly hall on the lower floor. At 10:00 AM, a bell rang to commence the opening ceremony. First, the brass band played music, and everyone stood up to sing the party anthem. Chairman Wu Jingxiong read the President's last will and testament and performed the ceremonial rites. The chairman first congratulated the nation on its unification and wished the members health. He then explained the Zhongshe's objectives, which are to promote the balanced development of moral, physical, intellectual, and aesthetic education. The undertakings promoted by the Zhongshe are based on these four aspects. Although the current facilities are rudimentary, future development will require the efforts of all members. He then expressed gratitude to Mr. Zhang Ganru, who provided funding for the construction of the premises and waived the rent, and to Mr. Li Gufan, who worked tirelessly for the Zhongshe, on behalf of the members.

Speeches were then given by Zi Min, Min, Yang Zi, and Wu Mai. The meeting adjourned at 11:00 AM. At noon, the first members' meeting and luncheon were held, chaired by Mr. Chen Fangzhi, who reported on the preparations and proposed the addition of Zhang Weici and Xu Yongzuo as directors, Zhang Jiongbo and Wang Xin as members of the Economic Committee, and Qu Jigang and Guo Waihui as members of the Club Committee. He also proposed the election of He Dekui, Chen Huaizhong, Li Gufan, Wang Renjing, and Sheng Zhuoshan as members of the Consumer Cooperative Committee, and Wang Yunwu, Wu Jingxiong, Pan Guangdan, Pan Gongzhan, and Zhong Ketuo as members of the Customs Reform Research Committee. Subsequently, Mr. Ma Xiangbo and Mr. Lu Zhixue delivered speeches. After the luncheon, which ended at 2:00 PM, entertainment began in the hall on the second floor, featuring performances by the string orchestra of Jinan University and the China Harmonica Association. The event concluded at 4:30 PM. At 7:00 PM that evening, a New Year's celebration was held, with Mr. Wu Zhihui delivering a humorous speech before dinner, which elicited laughter from the audience. After dinner, there were piano, vocal, and ensemble performances by Zhong Muzhen, Yu Yuese, and Yu Xiufang. The event concluded at midnight.

Reactionary Case of the Red Flag Daily 95

Undertaken by the Daye Printing House on Yalu Road 96

The Red Flag Daily, a reactionary publication, had long been banned by the authorities, but its printer remained unknown, allowing it to continue publishing on schedule. It has now been discovered by the Zhabei Police Department that the newspaper was printed by the Daye Printing House, located at 67 Yalu Road, Hongkou, founded by Qian Jinkan from Shaoxing. At 8:30 AM on the 9th, Chinese and Western detectives, some disguised as drivers, drove to the printing house to search it. Upon arriving at the entrance, they saw Qian's brother, Jin Gao, taking a bundle of over four thousand copies of the Red Flag Daily from inside, intending to transport them elsewhere. The detectives immediately intercepted him. Qian Jinkan's wife, Qian Chen, and hired laborers, Li Zhaochang, Liu Agen, Yang Enpei, and others, dared to rush out of the printing house to support Jin Gao and resist arrest, assaulting Detective Zhang Yousheng and Detective No. 96. Detective No. 96, seeing that these individuals were acting lawlessly, fired five shots into the air to subdue them. The detectives then entered the printing house and found a replica pistol, three seals, four thousand copies of the Red Flag Daily, and a set of type. Qian Jinkan and his associates, Cao Genfa, Hua Renliang, and Shi Risheng, who were hiding inside, were arrested. The following morning, they were sent to the Special District Local Court. Because the police department charged them under Articles 6 and 10 of the Anti-Revolutionary Act and Article 142 of the Criminal Code, the local court could not accept the case and transferred it to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court. Criminal Division Chief Song Zhisheng held a hearing and ordered the case to be adjourned for further verification. The defendants were then taken back to the detention center by the police.

The Forward March Team of Qinghefang 97

Caused by Dispatching for Service Without Pay 98

Xu Zhijiang, from Zhejiang, claiming to be commissioned by the Commander-in-Chief of the Army, Navy, and Air Force as the temporary commander of the Third Division of the First Forward March Team of the Anti-Rebellion Army, resided at Room 205, Qinghe Hotel, Qinghefang, Zhejiang Road. Because the military situation was unsettled, Chen Yefa, who resided at 823 Qiujiang Road, Baoshan Road, joined Xu's force. Chen was assigned by Xu as a special agent, but for several months, he was never dispatched for service or received any salary. Chen suspected that Xu was impersonating a military officer to defraud him of money and reported him to the Public Safety Bureau. The bureau chief dispatched detectives to cooperate with the Zhabei Police Department and secretly arrested Xu Zhijiang. Yang Wenjie, the chief of staff of the division, and Huang Hongbin, the boxing instructor of the First Regiment of the Central Military Police, who were in the same room as Xu, were also detained and sent to the Special District Local Court. The presiding judge interrogated them and ordered them to be detained for further investigation.

Fire at Qin Feng Silk Weaving Factory 99

The Qin Feng Silk Weaving Factory, located at 162 Route du Père Robert, in the French Concession, and owned by Shun Xianzhi, suddenly caught fire at 4:52 AM yesterday. Sparks flew onto the silk yarn and merchandise on the rear floor, which were instantly engulfed in flames. One floor was also destroyed. The French Concession Fire Brigade, along with the Nanshi Fire Brigade, dispatched vehicles to the scene to extinguish the fire. However, due to the cold weather and freezing water, rescue efforts were difficult. The fire was finally extinguished at 6:00 AM, with an estimated loss of five to six thousand yuan, including silk fabrics and building damage.

Deaths 100

Monk Lin Fell and Died 101

Monk Lin, a 19-year-old copper tax collector at the Dahua Motor Vehicle Company in Nanshi Guanqiao, fell from a high place while repairing a truck at the company the other day, sustaining severe injuries. He was taken to Shanghai Hospital, where he died. The local chief of the Sixteenth Ward reported the death to the Local Court for inspection. The deceased's father, Lin Amao, also applied to the hospital for exemption from inspection.

Unidentified Male Pauper Froze to Death 102

The weather has been unusually cold in recent days. The other night, an unidentified man in his twenties froze to death in Lujiazui, Pudong. He was scantily clad and obviously a pauper. Yesterday, Xie Along, the local head of the Twenty-Fourth Ward, reported the death to the Local Court for inspection.

Woman Fell into River and Froze to Death 103

The body of a woman in her twenties was found in the river along Longhua Road the other day. She was wearing a single layer of blue cloth and had a bun in her hair. She had no family. Sun Yongzhang, the local head of the First Ward, reported the death to the Local Court for inspection. The inspection revealed that she had accidentally fallen into the river and frozen to death. The body was taken to the hall for burial and sealed in a coffin, awaiting family identification. The woman appeared to be a pauper who had lost her footing due to the severe cold and fallen into the river.

Achievements of Tongren Fu Yuan Hall and its Branch 104

Hunan News reports that Tongren Fu Yuan Hall, Shanghai's only charitable organization, is well-managed and has significantly benefited the local community. In order to promote public understanding and awareness, the hall has released a report on the total number of coffins provided each month. According to the statistics for December of last year: 1) Tongren Fu Yuan Hall provided 78 large coffins and 93 small coffins to the New Puyutang, 26 large coffins to the Jiangsu Second Prison, and 24 large coffins and 39 small coffins to hospitals and at the gate. It buried 99 large coffins and 222 small coffins. 2) The French Concession branch provided 54 large coffins and 102 small coffins. It buried 59 large coffins and 254 small coffins. 3) The Tongren Fu Yuan Hall Rescue Bureau provided 2 large coffins and 61 small coffins. It buried 9 large coffins and 118 small coffins. The above statistics show that a total of 184 large coffins and 295 small coffins were provided in one month, and 167 large coffins and 594 small coffins were buried. The burial sites are located in the cemetery at Liuli Bridge in Pudong, each marked with the deceased's name, awaiting family identification.

The French Concession Tongren Fu Yuan Branch specializes in collecting and burying unidentified bodies from roadsides, hospitals, prisons, and other places within the French Concession, as well as collecting abandoned children's bodies and providing coffins year-round. It is now the 70th anniversary of its founding. Since Mr. Qin Shounong took over as director of the hall last spring, he has made great efforts to reorganize it, such as adding vehicles for transporting bodies, revising work regulations, and taking over the collection of unidentified bodies from hospitals in the Public Concession. Its achievements have been widely praised. It is reported that the hall's annual expenses have increased by about 10,000 yuan, with the coffin provision program requiring 5,000 yuan annually, and the burial of large and small bodies exceeding 5,000. The number does not include those who have families who provide their own coffins for burial.

The authorities encourage and promote this charitable undertaking, and benevolent people offer assistance and donations. The French Concession authorities, including the French Consul General's Office, the French Municipal Council, and the French Public Court, are enthusiastic about promoting charitable affairs within the concession and provide annual funding of 4,000 yuan. Furthermore, generous benefactors have donated approximately 400 yuan. The Siming Public Association donates 60 large wooden coffins annually (divided into three installments of 20 coffins each), with other items not included. This can truly be described as a dedication to public service and universal compassion. All sectors of society express their admiration and gratitude, which is worthy of recording. Additionally, the vehicles used by the hall's staff for official business, as well as the trucks and bicycles used to transport coffins and collect children's bodies, are issued permits by the Public Works Departments of both the English and French Concessions free of charge year-round, demonstrating their sincere commitment to philanthropy and promoting harmony. In 1930, a total of 677 large coffins and 4,613 small coffins were buried, totaling 5,390 coffins of all sizes, which were transported for burial to the tomb area in Pudong.

Business News Sudden Increase in Financial Interest Rates 110

Yesterday was Sunday, so the market was usually slow. However, the interest rates suddenly increased sharply. The early market rate was 7 qian 2 fen 1 li 3 hao 7 hu ban, while the afternoon market rate rose to 7 qian 2 fen 2 li 2 hao ban. As a result, it was almost 2 li higher than the early market rate the day before. The wind of the past was very strong, but yesterday's rise was not weak. The transactions made were 620,000 banknotes in the morning market and only 25,000 in the afternoon market. The outside market banknotes were 50,000 in the morning market and 70,000 in the afternoon market. The silver interest rate also rose. The early market rate was 1 qian 3 fen, while the afternoon market rate was 1 qian 2 fen, which was 7 to 8 fen higher than the afternoon market rate the day before. Bank collection and transactions were suspended due to the holiday. Money changers collected more than 3.3 million silver foreign exchange and more than 3.4 million silver public exchange. Small money changers exchanged more than 400,000 banknotes and more than 300,000 remittances from various places.

Public Debt Market Conditions at the Beginning of the National Calendar 115

Bond Prices Initially Fell, Then Strengthened, But Ultimately Trended Weak 116

Market Conditions Were Good, with Transactions Exceeding 44 Million 117

An examination of the market conditions for various bonds in Shanghai since the beginning of the National Calendar reveals that futures trading has been active. On Wednesday and Thursday, trading volumes reached 9 million yuan each day. On Tuesday and the weekend, trading volumes reached 6.8 to 6.9 million yuan each day. Only Monday was relatively flat. The price fluctuations were greater than at the end of the previous year. From Monday to Wednesday, sellers flooded the market, and demand was weak, causing bond prices to fall. The disarmament, demobilization, 1921 Customs, 1921 Relief, Consolidated Six, and other bonds fell significantly. The surge in gold prices and the chaos in international exchange rates widened the gap between gold and silver prices. Although the national fixed tariffs have been implemented, their impact on future customs revenues is likely to be significant, causing anxiety among market participants. On Thursday, bond prices had fallen significantly, and buyers became slightly more active, causing prices to rise across the board. The trend gradually stabilized over the weekend, and although prices continued to rise, the gains were small. As a result, prices generally retreated from the end of the previous year. The Consolidated Six and Disarmament bonds fell by as much as 2 yuan, and other bonds fell by smaller amounts. Total transaction volume for the week was 44.451 million, with 1921 Customs and Disarmament bonds being the most active, accounting for 11.71 million and 11.475 million yuan respectively. 1921 Relief bonds accounted for 6.885 million yuan, Demobilization bonds accounted for 5.955 million yuan, 1927 Public Bonds accounted for 5.11 million yuan, Consolidated Six bonds accounted for 2.055 million yuan, and other bonds were minimal.

Specifics were: Customs Bonds 730,000 yuan, 1919 Bonds 350,000 yuan, 1918 Bonds 200,000 yuan, Financial Bonds 25,000 yuan, Disaster Relief 10,000 yuan, and the rarely traded Bonds of 1915 also traded for 5,000 yuan. Spot trading was minimal, with total transaction volume for the week at 143,900 yuan. 1921 Customs bonds accounted for 92,100 yuan, Demobilization and Disarmament bonds accounted for over 20,000 yuan each, Disaster Relief bonds accounted for 16,000 yuan, and other bonds accounted for only a few thousand yuan each. The following table lists the high, low, and changes in prices for various bonds over the past week. All bonds except the Disaster Relief and 1918 bonds include both principal and interest. Analysis of the Surge in Cotton Yarn and Cotton Prices Last Week 118

Driving Force: Erratic Exchange Rates 119

Margin Calls 120

The dramatic rise in the cotton yarn market last week, during the New Year holiday, was unprecedented in recent times. This was due to the possibility of a one-and-a-half-month extension for money changers to settle accounts, which eased financial constraints, and the fact that factory exit taxes had not yet been implemented, allowing each bale of yarn to reach its destination without incurring 5-6 taels in taxes. As a result, traders vigorously sought supplies and urged the prompt shipment of existing stock. This had already improved the situation from last year. At the beginning of this year, the exchange rate fluctuated wildly, and gold prices soared, causing cotton prices to rise sharply, and the yarn market followed suit. Sellers were uneasy about this situation, and small investors were forced to cover their short positions, leading to this intense surge in the market. The pressure on sellers was too great, and the favorable news exacerbated the situation. Fortunately, Chaozhou and Japanese traders had not yet covered their short positions. The price of yarn for each month was 5-6 taels higher than last year, and the number of transactions was approximately 230,000 bales. Detailed figures will be provided later. Traders purchased approximately 7-8,000 bales of spot yarn this week. Traders purchased approximately 6-70,000 bales of forward yarn. Therefore, the bullish forces are very strong. Currently, the bulls and bears are fiercely competing. However, the overseas yarn market is average, and the market is temporarily still in a state of turmoil. It is feared that fluctuations may be unpredictable.

The surge in the cotton market last week was driven by fluctuations in foreign exchange rates, which caused the combined price of foreign cotton to rise sharply in relation to the Chinese currency. Local spot supplies were weak, and there was a lack of sources from various regions. Buyers intended to force sellers to cover their short positions. Therefore, the market secretly rose. In December, the margin calls reached 5 taels, and sellers were very hesitant. This year, gold prices have soared, and the short positions have increased dramatically, causing panic among small investors, who covered their positions at any cost, causing prices to rise from 2.7 qian to 5.3 qian. During these six days, the daily transaction volume was approximately 70,000 to 80,000 dan. This situation was due to the lack of deliverable standard goods and the large number of short positions. Although foreign cotton was weak, sellers were unprepared, and once the situation erupted, it was difficult to sustain. The price of each month was 2 taels higher than last year.

Spot Cotton: Factories were slightly more active, with sources including 1,500 bales of Tongzhou cotton, 2,000 bales of Yao cotton, and 1,050 bales of Dongtai cotton. Factories purchased 23,365 dan, and trading companies purchased 2,200 dan. The volume of purchases by each factory is recorded below.

Grain: The Rice Market Remains Stable Despite the Cold Weather 122

The weather yesterday in Zhabei was extremely cold and freezing, resulting in a significant reduction in supplies from the Lu Li Road. Sales in all directions were also sluggish on the 10th or so. The price of the special top grade remained at 13 yuan 8 jiao, while the market price was only around 13 yuan 5 jiao. The overall trend can be described as stable. The arrival and sales of thin tao were both sluggish, with no gains or losses. The best-selling rice was sheep xiang, with zero gut being especially popular. Prices were stable. The top grade was about to reach 13 yuan. The price of Du bu xiang was not as vibrant as sheep xiang, but the market shape was still active. Prices were consistent and stable. The supply of bian yuan he was limited, and sales were sluggish. The situation was stable. The day's trading was light, with little fluctuation in prices and a slight increase in transaction volume.

Yesterday, the supply from rivers to Shanghai South was scarce. West and south roads saw few arrivals. Chang geng continued to be in short supply, so the price of 13 yuan for goods on the market was considered the market peak. However, in reality, special geng required 13 yuan 3-4 jiao. Suzhou and Tongzhou special geng was rare, and sales were sluggish. Store gut were flat, and country sales were also weak. It was generally not easy to raise prices. However, the consecutive cold days inevitably led to firmness. The buying of early thin dao and early rice in the southern area was light. Very few Yong gu were imported. The market was tight, and the market situation was clearly stable. The price of high-quality sheep du was firm, while the price of middle and lower-quality goods was stagnant. The supply of bai yuan he was not abundant, and there were few top-quality goods. Therefore, the price of tong bian barely held steady, while the price of yin hua slightly declined.

Sharp Drop in New Year's Standard Soybeans 123

Increased by Three Qian Before Halftime, Then Recouped Due to Gold Price 124

The opening price of the Red Board Standard Futures Soybean was soft because of the unexpected changes that took place in Dalian. Stockowners were frantically throwing out beans for each period which caused the price to sharply reverse direction. This move roused panic in the hearts of the local gang of brokers and those from the interior. Old bull orders and new short orders went out together with weakness in the market such as had never been seen before. The price slid down to more than three qian in two days with sales reaching more than 400 cars. At this time, the market's eye was unanimously on four liang. After the situation settled on Wednesday, there was a slight covering of earlier short positions. Prices strengthened slightly. After that, on Thursday, the price suddenly turned around because margin rates were ceaselessly rising and at the same time Western brokerages in Dalian were showing interest and starting to move up. This made everyone happy. Homes continued to cover and oil manufacturers and carters began to buy. Prices proceeded tightly till over the weekend when, because of a telegram from Dalian reporting prices up by a jiao, the situation became very active. Buying became open and unobstructed. Nearby and later contracts all rose by 7-8 fen and the price opened up the barrier of 4 liang 5 qian. The volume of exchange transactions has already greatly increased and has now reached over 2000 cars. Parties everywhere have been paying increased attention to the bean market. New Year's Sugar Market: Meng Jin Has Not Yet Recovered 126

Highest Price since the Start of the Year: Japanese Sugar Stepping Upward 127

Local Ice Has Risen Again Three Qian: However, Trading in Board Lots Has Quieted Down 128

Since the sugar market opened on the 5th, after the New Year's holidays, it has been rising because international prices have gone up and production areas have reported rising wind. Merchants everywhere have said that since customs duties in the interior have been recalled, purchases have been surging ahead and the atmosphere is even better. Every type of sugar has been taking flight and flourishing. Raw sand and white prices are above 10 liang, which is the highest price since the start of the year. Dutch Red is also tracking this and now costs more than 9 liang. Ice flower and clear are also above 9 liang 2 qian. The rise in local ice is even sharper and has risen to 12 liang 6 qian. Japanese sugar is also stepping up higher, and even though a great deal of goods are arriving at the end of the year, this hasn't had the slightest impact on the market atmosphere because demand has been quite strong and where people's desires are, prices are surging high. 8-number three-heat-and-a-half has reached its highest price of 10 liang 07 qian, and prices compared to the end of the year are already up more than 1 liang which is a record for the sugar market at the start of the year.

At yesterday's market draw made by the guild, the atmosphere for 24-Number Dutch raw sugar was quite strong at first with demand still vigorous. The price for transactions was 10 liang 6 qian ban, and the buying and selling of Hong Kong goods at 10 liang 05 qian ban was still busy. After this, because spot prices on the board lot were abundant, the later market was leveled off a bit as a result. 20-Number middle-sand white cost 10 liang, which was also not remarkable. The price of 8-Number Dutch Red at 9 liang 2 qian ban was quite sprightly. Japanese sugar was also showing price steps. N Mark was at 10 liang 08 qian ban and was still running out. Y T Mark was at 10 liang 06 qian ban to 7 qian. Y P Mark was at 11 liang 1 qian and bright China goods were at 11 liang. Y P O Mark was at 10 liang 02 qian to 2 qian ban. The market atmosphere was firm and still up a qian compared to before. Local ice prices were up by 3 qian because manufacturers everywhere were announcing quite a lot of ice. The Shanghai factory announced that Jen Character Ice was selling for 13 liang 9 qian and Dry Character was at 13 liang 8 qian. The Zhonghua factory announced that Zhong Character ice was selling for 13 liang 9 qian and a large bag of ice was selling for 13 liang 2 qian. These two houses each reported selling over 1000 packages. The new factory Guohua sold 700 packages at the same price. Markets everywhere were agile. There was no trade because prices were being cried up high in board lots for all colors. The asking price for ice flower clear was 10 liang. The asking price for new clear sugar was 8 liang 2 qian but there were still few offers. Huaxin company opened up and announced that they had 3000 sacks of spot raw white with a price of 10 liang 06 qian ban.

Ceremony for the Completion of the New Liangjiang Girls' School Building 132

The Liangjiang Girls' Physical Education School on Daji Road held a ceremony at 10:00 AM on New Year's Day to commemorate the tenth anniversary of the completion of its new school building. More than 600 people attended, including Director Pan Gongzhan of the Social Affairs Bureau and Ma Chonggan. Chairman Ma Xiangbo of the board of directors, on behalf of the board, delivered a speech. Commissioner Chu Minyi also delivered a speech on behalf of the school board. Certificates were presented to the ninth graduating class of teachers. Principal Lu Lihua gave a reply. Speeches were given by representatives of administrative organs and members of the school board, all of which were encouraging and emphasized practical application. The auditorium had two floors, with a vertical scroll personally written by Ma Xiangbo and a couplet presented by Director Pan Gongzhan hanging on the walls. Beside the auditorium on the left was a tea room. The four walls were covered with inscriptions and poems by presidents of various colleges, ministers of various departments, chairmen of various provinces, directors of provincial departments, the mayor of this city, the Songhu Garrison Commander, and directors of various bureaus. There were also horizontal plaques from renowned figures in the education field such as Huang Yanpei, Shen Enfu, Jiang Hengyuan, Jiang Weiqiao, and Wang Xishen. Several silver-framed mirrors were presented by figures from the press such as Ge Gongzhen. The third and fourth floors were student dormitories, designed in a village style with sixteen "villages." The lowest level was for offices and reception rooms, displaying various awards received over the years, enlarged photographs of Principal Lu Lihua and the basketball team, and over a hundred frames of animated viewing photographs. Outside, there was a library and a piano room. In the corridor, there was a personally inscribed school motto by Wang Yibo, and the latest portraits gifted by Chairman Jiang and Minister He of the Military Administration Department. The lower level of the second school building was a harmonium room and a bathhouse, with a cooperative society beside it. The upper floors were all classrooms and each piano room had a view of the sports field. The foundations for the gymnasium and swimming pool to be built were also located there. It is said that within a few days of the school opening, more than 400 visitors had come to visit. President Zhang Boling of Nankai University also made a special trip to visit, and Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting also sent a congratulatory telegram.

The City Executive Committee Asks for Swift Handling of the Guanghua University Incident 133

(Guomin News Agency) The Guanghua University incident in this city has been ongoing for more than a month. It is now reported that the Municipal Executive Committee yesterday submitted another report to the Central Government requesting prompt action and also sent a letter inviting the university president to the city government for a discussion. The oppressed students of the university are still actively fighting. Yang Shuchun, a student who was expelled, issued a declaration yesterday providing a factual account of the university incident.

Shao Lizi Appointed as Director of Fudan Experimental Middle School 134

Xu Zeye Appointed as Secretary

The position of director of Fudan Experimental Middle School, which had been vacant since Chen Wangdao’s departure, has finally been decided. The university's board of directors has appointed Shao Lizi as the director of the middle school. Shao has hired Xu Zeye, a talented graduate of Fudan University, as his secretary. It is reported that Xu previously served as a secretary to the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau and as head of the Fourth Division. He has taught at National Zhejiang University, Shanghai College of Politics and Law, and other schools for many years. He assumed his duties on January 6. It is said that there will be no major changes to the internal faculty and staff. From now on, the school can embark on a path of active development, which is cause for celebration for the school.

Chinese Art Academy Opens Painting and Calligraphy Exhibition 135

Yesterday was the third day of the painting and calligraphy exhibition at the Chinese Art Academy on Qiqi Road in this city. The venue was filled with exquisite works by teachers, students, and renowned artists from across the country, a truly beautiful sight. The weather cleared up after the snow, and the number of visitors reached over three thousand. Most of them were painters, calligraphers, and connoisseurs, who expressed high praise for the exquisite quality of the exhibits. It is reported that the exhibition will move to the Suzhou-Nanjing area tomorrow.

White Goose 136

Painting Research Institute to Hold Exhibition

The 5th Practice Exhibition of White Goose Painting Research Institute should have been held at the end of the 19th year of the Republic era. However, the affairs of the institute will have major improvements and expansions from the spring term of this year. In order to have a long-term consideration of various new plans, the exhibition had to be postponed. At the same time, considering the shallow impression of general vocational school achievement exhibitions, we are even more unwilling to hastily deal with it by mixing in it. The institute is a painting research group founded in Shanghai. Although the history is only two years, the spirit is strict and the achievements are unique. It has long enjoyed a good reputation in society. The cooperative preparations and the 5th practice paintings are even more seen only in previous exhibitions. It is reported that the exhibition date is scheduled for around the 20th of this month, and a strict review and display of each painting is underway.

Junyi Middle School Adds Branch School 137

Junyi Middle School, founded by Wu Kaixian and others from the Municipal Committee on Guohuo Road in this city, has been progressing rapidly in the past two years. The number of students has increased sharply to around six hundred this semester. Principal Pan Gongzhan believes that it will be difficult to complete the new school building in a short period of time, so if he wants to accommodate so many students, he can only temporarily rent a branch school. It is reported that the school has rented ten new houses next to the school. Because everything needs to be arranged, the school's Academic Affairs Director Huang Zaoxiong, General Affairs Director Zhou Yongnan, Moral Education Director Huang Xuchu, and High School Directors He Ziguo and Luo Yingxiong are quite busy purchasing equipment for the additional classes.

The Severe Cold Does Not Diminish the Enthusiasm of Soccer Fans 139

After the heavy snow, the weather suddenly turned cold, and everyone thought that the competition would not be held. However, it proceeded as usual. Since both teams are the most famous teams in Shanghai, soccer fans were not afraid of the severe cold and flocked to Shen Garden, with about a thousand people. The cold wind cut their faces, and the cold air pierced their bones, but they still sat precariously to enjoy the soccer skills. It can be said that they are truly fans.
